Current Affairs Commentary

Briand Goes to Geneva

In countries with a parliamentary system, the key lies in the cabinet. If the cabinet is competent, it will harmonize with the parliament internally and cooperate with friendly nations externally. Only then can the country's position be consolidated. Although the president sits majestically on top, in reality, their influence is not as significant as that of a key figure in the cabinet. However, people are often dazzled by the president's superficial glory and exhaust the strength of their party and faction to compete for the position. No one has ever willingly given it up. However, in the recent French presidential election, the left wing wanted to maintain Foreign Minister Briand's position and allow him to continue his long-standing foreign policy. Therefore, they used secret ballots to defeat him. But Briand did not resign in disappointment due to the defeat. Now he is resolutely going to Geneva to deal with the League of Nations meeting. This also shows that people's thinking has advanced to reality and is not obsessed with the president's superficial glory. Today, France's position in foreign affairs is most important. Major issues concerning international relations and world security are now awaiting resolution at the Geneva Conference, and the direction of France's foreign policy is particularly crucial. Therefore, after the results of this election were announced, representatives from various countries participating in the parliament focused on Briand's actions. Those who previously expressed sympathy for Briand's foreign policy all praised him for not being concerned about personal gains and losses and for being worthy of a great political figure. We observe the current world situation, and Briand's departure or stay is indeed very important to the future of the European situation. The French political parties are willing to sacrifice the most honorable presidential title to implement their foreign policy, which is truly commendable among today's political parties.

Receiving Important Telegrams from Home

(Nanjing) The drafting committee for the declaration on receiving the Prime Minister's legacy convened a meeting on the afternoon of the 15th. The draft has been finalized and will be reported to the General Assembly immediately. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Military Parade Today

(Nanjing) At 9 AM on the 16th, the National Government invited representatives of the National Congress to review the troops at the airfield and cordially invited foreign guests to observe. A rostrum was set up in the center of the field, with spectator stands on both sides, each ten meters high. All arrangements and furnishings were extremely luxurious and magnificent. More than 400 seats were arranged. The troops to be reviewed included the infantry, cavalry, artillery, machine gun, and tank units of the First Guard Division. They were all scheduled to complete assembly by 7 AM. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Overseas Chinese Representatives Call on Chiang

(Nanjing) Overseas Chinese representatives Zheng Zhannan, Chen Renyi, Huang Dingzhi, Chen Zhaoqi, Wu Xiaozhu, and Sen Die called on Chiang at noon on the 15th and talked for a long time. Chiang inquired very earnestly about the situation of the overseas Chinese and invited the representatives to dine together. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

National Press Circle Hosts a Banquet for National Congress Representatives

Pan Gongbi Delivers Welcome Speech

(Nanjing) The national press circle held a banquet at the Central Gymnasium (National Congress Representatives Banquet Hall) at 6 PM on the afternoon of the 15th to welcome all the representatives of the National Congress, members of the Central Committee, and members of the National Government, totaling more than 300 people. Chairman Pan Gongbi delivered a welcome speech. Shao YuanChong, Liu Luyin, and representative Yan Hongzhu all gave sincere speeches. Pan Gongbi's speech is as follows:

"Colleagues in the press circle sincerely welcome all the gentlemen attending the National Congress. Colleagues in the press circle in Nanjing have been admiring your style and listening to your high-level discussions in the National Congress for days. We are deeply pleased to have you gather here tonight despite your busy schedules. The National Congress has been convened for exactly ten days. In these ten days, you have passed the Provisional Constitution for the Period of Political Tutelage, declared the abolition of unequal treaties, and decided on various major policy plans, making great contributions to the country and the people. You gentlemen are national representatives, and my colleagues dare not claim to be representatives of the people to thank you. But my colleagues are also citizens, and how can we not express our deep gratitude? You come from overseas, from Mongolia and Tibet, from various provinces and cities. Although the title of representative you hold is only temporary, the reason why you were elected as representatives must be because your talents, virtues, and integrity are admired by all. Those who are admired by all, even without a title, are in fact leaders of society. Therefore, my colleagues hope that your role as representatives of the National Congress is important and great, but we hope that your role as social leaders is even further and more important. My colleagues in the press circle select materials and discuss matters from different perspectives, seeing benevolence and wisdom, and our views are not entirely the same. But there are two points on which we are consistent. First, we hope for peace and unification, and we believe that peace and unification must be consolidated by the strong power of the people. Looking at the strong and prosperous countries of modern times, they have not had internal strife for a long time, which is enviable. Is this because of the wisdom of their governments, or because of the strong power of the people? If it is said that it is because of the wisdom of the government, is it accidental, fate, or is it because the people have the power to prevent the existence of an unwise government? Looking at the endless internal strife in our country, is it not lamentable? However, from the perspective of the people, who does not hate chaos? Despite the hatred of chaos, the chaos continues, is it not because the people who hate chaos have no power at all? My colleagues firmly believe that the National Government has the power to quell chaos, but what the people seek is definitely not quelling chaos, but no chaos. The method to seek no chaos is definitely not for the government and army to suppress the whole country, but for the people to have a strong power at any time and any place, so that chaos cannot occur. In other words, those who want to create chaos are afraid of the power of the people and dare not create chaos, until they do not want to create chaos. Therefore, it is said that peace and unification must begin with increasing the power of the people. On this point, my colleagues feel that we have the responsibility to promote and publicize it, while the actual work of increasing the power of the people is still up to you gentlemen. This is the first belief of my colleagues and the first wish for you. Second, my colleagues believe that in principle, it is difficult for the government to satisfy everyone. This is the same in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. In fact, the achievements of today's National Government are also difficult to satisfy everyone. However, my colleagues consider the oppression of the international community, the lessons of history, the difficulties of the country, and the exhaustion of people's livelihood, and deeply feel that the National Government is worthy of support and must be supported, and supported for the sake of the people, not for the sake of the government. My colleagues believe that supporting the government from the perspective of the press is definitely not blind praise, but is based on well-intentioned criticism to promote the functions of governments at all levels. This is the most appropriate and effective method of support. Because the government has the greatest functions, it is the most solid government. This is the second belief of my colleagues, and it is your responsibility to practically assist the functions of governments at all levels. This is the second wish of my colleagues for you. People regard public opinion as the representative of the people. My colleagues dare not be self-deprecating, and often regard ourselves as the representatives of the people. Tonight, we are meeting the representatives elected by the people in the capital, and we cannot help but feel inferior. However, my colleagues consider the basis for the existence of public opinion and the mission that public opinion bears, and we will still say what the people want to say and say what the people should say, and claim to be representatives of the people. Are we representing the people, or are you representing the people? Although the nature and position are different, at least all those present are great citizens of the great Republic of China. The two points mentioned above are the responsibility of my colleagues, the responsibility of you gentlemen, and what is not the responsibility of the people? Increasing the power of the people also depends on the guidance and encouragement of the government, and assisting the functions of the government also depends on the government's openness and tolerance. This is especially hoped for the members of the Central Committee and the members of the National Government present today. I respectfully offer you a glass of wine, and let us all drink it."

Important Proposal Contents: Case to Cancel Harsh Treatment of Overseas Chinese

(Nanjing) Zheng Zhan-nan and 54 others propose urgently negotiating with various countries' governments to cancel harsh treatment of overseas Chinese. Measures: (1) Whenever various countries' governments promulgate various harsh treatment regulations against overseas Chinese, the government should earnestly negotiate for their cancellation. (2) For countries whose governments have not yet signed treaties with China, treaties of equality and mutual benefit should be promptly established to allow overseas Chinese to develop freely under treaty protections. (3) The government should carefully select consular appointees stationed in various regions in the future, appointing those with suitable talents, enabling them to argue based on reason against the harsh treatment regulations promulgated by various governments. For consuls already dispatched who cannot seek benefits for overseas Chinese and are opposed by overseas Chinese, the government should immediately recall them and appoint replacements. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

Developing the Northwest and Handling Relief Through Labor

(Nanjing) Li Fan-yi and 68 others propose developing the Northwest and handling relief through labor to seek construction and rescue the people from disaster. Measures: (A) The focus of this case is on developing the Northwest, and

Page 9

Receiving Important Domestic Telegrams

to use the capital for developing the Northwest to organize relief through labor. In other words, it means utilizing disaster victims in the Northwest to engage in Northwest construction. (B) It is found that the consumption of cigarettes has become a huge drain on the country. Young men and women arbitrarily smoke, which harms the nation's health and corrupts national morality. The harm cannot be overstated. According to precise statistics, the national consumption of cigarettes alone amounts to a staggering 200 million yuan annually. It is proposed that this conference inform the National Government and instruct the Ministry of Finance to increase the current tax rate by 30 percent, which would yield 60 million yuan. This would be used as a fund to issue 60 million yuan in public bonds for national disaster relief, with 30 million yuan allocated specifically for developing the Northwest. This fund would be used to organize beneficial relief through labor, combining prohibition with taxation. This would not only curb the decadent habits of young people but also be used for productive construction, achieving two goals with one move, and nothing could be better than this. As for cigarette tax rates, the amounts levied in other countries are excessive. Even with our country's increase, it is still far from the tax rates of other countries. Contemporary scholars have discussed this in great detail, so there is no need to elaborate further.

Establishing Mongolian Education Programs

(Nanjing) Wu He-ling and 182 others propose that the central government allocate special funds and encourage the establishment of Mongolian education and various cultural undertakings. Measures: (1) The central government should allocate special funds and actively establish Mongolian education according to the established plan. (2) The central government should formulate reward measures to encourage Mongolians to independently establish education and various cultural undertakings. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

Guaranteeing Mongolian Leagues and Banners

(Nanjing) Wu He-ling and 180 others propose guaranteeing Mongolian leagues and banners and the livelihood of Mongolians. Measures: (1) The governing rights of all Mongolian leagues and banners should remain as before. (2) Land in Mongolia unsuitable for cultivation should remain as pastures for Mongolians, and the central government should encourage the improvement of animal husbandry. Land suitable for cultivation should, when cultivated, first provide Mongolians with ample land for their livelihood and public school land. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

Relieving the Three Provinces of Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia

(Nanjing) Ma Fu-xiang and 149 others propose that the nation use its full strength to relieve the three provinces of Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia. The original text is as follows: Since unification was achieved and military affairs concluded, those who seek long-term stability and peace for the Party and the nation all say, "Develop the Northwest, manage the Northwest." Among the most powerful proposals is "Move troops to populate the border," which is a fundamental plan for consolidating national defense. From a superficial perspective, it seems to be well-founded and logically sound. However, after studying the actual situation of the three provinces, it is best to start with the economic construction of the three provinces, which is easy to implement quickly, achieving twice the results with half the effort. The government spends a limited amount, and the people benefit immensely. Specific relief measures are proposed, which are also the initial steps in the Northwest development plan. (1) The Baoning Railway should be completed ahead of schedule to facilitate transportation. Measure: Instruct the Ministry of Railways to complete it by a set deadline. (2) The aviation routes in Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia should be developed ahead of schedule. Measure: Instruct the Ministry of Communications to open air routes in Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia in the shortest possible time and to equip aircraft to facilitate civil aviation. (3) Developing water conservancy in the upper reaches of the Yellow River to avoid floods in the lower reaches of Henan and Shandong provinces. Large-scale measures should be taken in Ningxia and the Hetao region to dig canals and divert the river for irrigation. Measure: Request the government to designate special funds and instruct the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission to implement it by a set deadline. At a minimum, it should be planned and considered concurrently with the Huai River diversion project to achieve effective results. (4) Improve animal husbandry, agriculture, and forestry in Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia to enrich the people's livelihood. Measure: Instruct the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to use its full strength to develop water conservancy in the three provinces ahead of schedule, encourage afforestation, protect forests, develop animal husbandry, improve breeds of horses, cattle, and sheep, exploit mineral resources, and use local raw materials to establish factories. (5) Education in Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia should receive special attention to achieve universal education. Measure: Instruct the Ministry of Education to stipulate local education funding for the three provinces and, given the special circumstances of the three provinces, request special subsidies from the central government or designate special funds for education in the three provinces from the Boxer Indemnity funds to ensure practical implementation. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

Establishing an Economic Conference

(Nanjing) He Yu-fang and 54 others propose establishing an economic conference to resolve China's economic problems. (Measures) (1) The German Economic Council has a special clause in its constitution. Since China's constitution has not yet been established, it is advisable to formulate a special Economic Council Law or stipulate it first in the provisional constitution to include it in the constitution in the future and to serve as the basis for organizing the Economic Council now. (2) After Germany promulgated its constitution, it immediately began drafting laws for the organization of the Economic Council. Due to the urgency, it first promulgated the Provisional Economic Council Organization Law to convene it by a set deadline. China's economic problems urgently need to be resolved, so it is also advisable to first promulgate a type of Provisional Economic Council Law to meet the needs and facilitate convening. (3) The points that should be noted in the establishment of the Economic Council are that the mechanism for resolving economic problems must be independent, and the people resolving economic problems must be average in terms of occupation and even more so in terms of individuals. Based on these two points as the goal of organizing the Economic Council, the laws and resolutions passed by the council will have an independent spirit, and the various groups and classes gathered by the council will have opportunities for coordination. In this way, the tragedy of class struggle can be avoided, and international economic survival can be adapted.

Special Authorization for Outer Mongolian Autonomy

Wu He-ling's Proposal

(Nanjing) Wu He-ling and 173 others propose announcing to the country and abroad the special authorization for Outer Mongolian autonomy to achieve unification as soon as possible. Reasons and measures: Outer Mongolia is a part of China's territory, which has long been recognized by the world. At the end of the Qing Dynasty, the addition of new troops in Outer Mongolia caused suspicion among the Mongolians. Taking advantage of the Wuchang Uprising, they declared independence. By the fourth year of the Republic of China, considering the generous treatment of Inner Mongolia by the central government, they cancelled their independence and changed to autonomy, recognizing China's suzerainty and that Outer Mongolia was still China's territory. If the covenant had not been violated, it could have been a long-term solution. However, in the ninth year of the Republic of China, Xu Shu-zheng forcibly cancelled Outer Mongolian autonomy by deploying troops, which led to a reaction from Outer Mongolian officials and civilians and a declaration of a second independence. Since returning and leaving again and again, the enthusiasm of the people for their homeland has changed from hope to a mentality of turning away and leaving for good. The Soviet Russian imperialists took advantage of this weakness to spread their communist heresies, ultimately creating today's dangerous situation. The knowledgeable people of Outer Mongolia are not unaware that drinking poison will kill them, but to quench their immediate thirst, they have no choice but to endure bitterness. Although the ultimate goal of Soviet Russia is to swallow Outer Mongolia, its propaganda and measures all cater to the extreme ideas of Mongolian youth to sell their deceit, such as publicizing and guiding the establishment of an independent republic in Mongolia, sending Inner Mongolian students to study in Europe and America, providing military supplies to strengthen armaments, supplying machinery to establish various industries, and dispatching teachers to instill communist doctrines. At the same time, they vigorously publicize China's harsh treatment of Mongolia to provoke them. All of these are things that Mongolian youth are very happy to hear and very willing to promote. Once someone comes forward to assist them, how can they not regard it as kindness and be anesthetized by it? Although Soviet Russia's influence in Outer Mongolia is not yet fully consolidated, in recent years, it has greatly moved towards Inner Mongolia, such as directing Mongolian soldiers to plunder Inner Mongolian livestock, dispatching party members to Inner Mongolia to instigate and recruit young people to study in Outer Mongolia. If this continues unchecked, then in a few years, not only will the relationship between Soviet Russia and Outer Mongolia become closer and more difficult to eradicate, but also the various leagues and banners of Inner Mongolia, bordering the provinces, will inevitably lead to an unquenchable disaster due to the outward development of Russian and Mongolian violence. Moreover, the property and goods of Chinese businessmen in Outer Mongolia have now been confiscated, and calls for help are endless. People fleeing from Outer Mongolia describe the cruelty of communism and their earnest hope for China. However, because they do not know how China will treat them, they dare not return rashly. The situation is particularly heartbreaking to hear. At this time, when the National Assembly is jointly planning unification and construction, we cannot but urgently seek a proper solution to this major problem of hidden worries. After repeated consideration, the representatives believe that the reason why the people of Outer Mongolia are hesitant is partly due to Soviet Russia's misrepresentations and partly due to their doubts about our government. The urgent task now is to uphold our Party's advocacy of supporting small and weak nations to enable them to self-determine and self-govern, to grant Outer Mongolia autonomy, and to have the National Government stipulate support measures and announce them to China and abroad to show great faith. Then, based on this principle, engage in propaganda, so that the people of Outer Mongolia who love their motherland can return with peace of mind, and those anesthetized youths will also become aware of it due to the trend of the majority. In this way, through gradual management, the already missing territory can be restored to completeness. Otherwise, we are nurturing disaster and leaving endless troubles. The representatives come from Mongolia and have more accurate observations. We respectfully offer our humble suggestions and respectfully request a public decision. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

Continuing Yesterday's Resolution on Suppressing Bandits

(Nanjing) Fourth, producers in rural and urban areas must seek mutual benefit within the scope of legal protection based on the principle of labor-capital mutual assistance and coordination. The Red bandits, under the direction of red imperialists, are dedicated to destroying our country's rural and urban economies. Therefore, they lure farmers with slogans such as resisting rent and taxes and confiscating land, causing them to constantly engage in cruel struggles of murder and arson. They lure workers with slogans such as increasing wages, reducing working hours, and improving treatment, causing them to constantly engage in daily struggles that exceed the scope. The result of these two struggles is that, in reality, both the rural economy and the urban economy are in a state of bankruptcy, and the farmers and workers they utilize will also perish due to unemployment and displacement. The people of our country, especially the farmers and workers of our country, should know that the theories boasted by the Red bandits are completely unsuitable for China's actual economic situation. As far as the rural economy is concerned, the central theory boasted by the Red bandits is the land revolution, and the content of the land revolution is to equally divide the land. However, they do not know that China's land system was originally very equal. According to statistics in recent years, farmers with 10 to 20 mu of land account for 62% of the total cultivated land in the country, those with 30 mu or more account for 21%, those with 50 mu or more account for 11%, and those with 100 mu or more account for about 6%. It can be seen that the distribution of land in China is already so equal. At the same time, the changing state of land ownership of farmers with 10 to 50 mu of land has a tendency to increase, while the changing state of land ownership of farmers with 50 to 100 mu or more has only a trend of division and no trend of concentration. It can be seen that the change in land distribution in China still does not exceed its scope of equal balance. Therefore, it is clear that the Red bandits' theory of equally dividing land is not applicable to China. Moreover, the so-called equal division of land by the Red bandits, although superficially claiming to equally divide it according to population, in fact, they neither count the population nor count the land. How can they equally divide it? Even if there are local statistics, the population density of the country is different, and the breadth and fertility of the land are very different. How can the bandits equally divide it? If it is equally divided according to the population, it will inevitably lead to those who can cultivate the land having no land to use, and those who cannot cultivate the land having no people to use. Seeking equality in this way will result in the opposite. From this, it can be seen that the fallacies used by the Red bandits to incite farmers have been refuted in fact. Furthermore, in terms of the urban economy, our country's production is backward, and the capitalist system has not yet been formed. To deal with the powerful Western capitalist methods, adding them to the weak investors will not only destroy the production enterprises that are just beginning, but also cut off the lifeline of the workers themselves. This is a fact that the Red bandits have repeatedly tried and tested since the Wuhan terror era in the fifteenth year, without waiting for any other evidence. In recent years, workers have also known that economic struggles are enough to increase their own suffering, so they no longer believe in the fallacy of striking at every turn. The Red bandits have seen this psychology of their fellow countrymen, so they have changed their methods of incitement and advanced with the tactic of slowing down work. However, no matter how the Red bandits change their methods of inciting workers, the result is still to destroy our country's production enterprises, and the result is still that workers themselves will never have any improvement in their welfare. At the same time, because Chinese workers misuse economic struggles for the production enterprises of their own country, any large-scale production in their own country cannot be revitalized. As a result, foreign industries backed by strong Western capitalism are able to take advantage of the situation to invade China's territory. This phenomenon is particularly evident in Shanghai. From this, it can be seen that another result of Chinese workers' believing in economic struggles is to promote the transplantation of foreign capitalism into China. Therefore, the theories and methods relied upon by the Red bandits to deceive the workers of our country, once tried and used, will ultimately result in three kinds of disasters: first, the elimination of our country's production; second, the increase of unemployment among workers in our country; and third, the promotion of the invasion of foreign capitalism. In the eyes of the red imperialists, they have been seeking these disasters that harm China's economic life day and night, but why are a few workers in our country willing to be tigers and not realize it? To sum up the theories and methods of the red imperialists' instigating their bandits to lure farmers and workers, their intention is to destroy our country's rural and urban economies. It is obvious that from now on, the farmers and workers of our country must thoroughly understand that this method of the Red bandits, which destroys social and economic life, is inappropriate. They must each follow the principle of labor-capital mutual assistance and coordination to engage in increasing production and improving production skills. Only by striving to increase production can production enterprises continue to develop, only by the continuous development of production enterprises can the interests of farmers and workers continue to increase, their lives can continue to improve, and their skills can continue to improve. If they do the opposite and do not strive to increase production, but seek to increase benefits, improve their lives, and improve their skills, there will be no escape from the situation where labor and capital perish together. Now, the principle of labor-capital mutual coordination has been established as one of the fundamental policies of the national economy, and the state is also based on this principle, formulating various laws and regulations to protect the interests of farmers and workers, in the hope that all the people involved in production enterprises in the country will jointly implement it in the future. This is not only the direction that must be taken to develop the national economy, but also the means to reverse the bad habits of those who have been misled by the Red bandits. This is another important meaning of our people's assisting the government in suppressing the disasters of the Red bandits in accordance with the principle of labor-capital mutual assistance and coordination within the scope of the law to seek the mutual benefits of both parties. (To be continued)

He Fei Is Still in Yuan'an

Zhang Zhi's Main Force Flees to Henan

(Hankou) A telegram from the Command Headquarters reports that He Fei is still in the territory of Yuan'an. The encirclement of the various troops has been completed. Guo's troops, Yuan, Wang, and Tong's regiments, have advanced from Xiema River to Shuiban in the territory of Yuan, and were the first to contact the bandit troops. The remaining troops are also advancing in separate directions and will launch a general attack. The Command Headquarters specially ordered Xu Yuanquan, Fan Shisheng, Zhao Guanying, Wang Guangzong, Guo Xun, and other three divisions and two brigades to be responsible for the encirclement and suppression, and to clear them before the 20th. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

(Hankou) Wang Lingji telegraphed on the 15th that the remnants of the Huang bandits were entrenched in Wansian Cave on the north bank of the Ba River and were captured by Zhang Jie's brigade on the 13th. The Huang bandits fled. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

(Hankou) Zhang Zhi, a large bandit force in northern Hubei, was defeated by Zhao Guanying's division and has fled to Henan. The Command Headquarters ordered Li Yunjie's troops to block them, while Zhao's troops moved to suppress He Long. It is heard that after He is cleared, they will open Huangmei Guangji for defense. (Fifteenth Dispatch)

Central Fiscal Situation

(Nanjing) Economic circles are concerned. Rumors are circulating about the government's financial difficulties,

Page 10

but these are not confirmed. One institution still has seven million in cash. As for the eighty million in customs treasury bonds, thirty million have already been sold on the Shanghai market, thirty million have been mortgaged for loans, and there are still twenty million remaining. Part of this can be used for post-war relief in the North. Calculating the funds from these customs treasury bonds, there is still a surplus that can be used for new guarantees. Combined with the four consolidated tax revenues, there will be enough in the future to guarantee eighty million treasury bonds. (15th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Panchen Lama plans to meet Chiang Kai-shek within the next few days to discuss ways to resolve the conflicts between Tibet and Kham. It is reported that Chiang advocates restoring the Dalai Lama to preside over the former Tibet and the Panchen Lama to preside over the latter Tibet. Furthermore, the central government should continue to send senior officials to investigate the truth, first to stop military actions, and to resolve all issues through political means. Bizarre Murder Case in the Capital

Naked Woman Killed

Perpetrator Drowns Himself

(Nanjing) At 3:00 AM on the 15th, a woman named Wang Caixi in Xijunyu Lane was stabbed to death in her bedroom. When her family discovered the crime, Caixi was lying naked, dead on the doorstep. As the family rushed to enter the room to investigate, they suddenly heard a splash from the window near the river. Someone had jumped into the Qinhuai River. Looking back at the bed, they saw it was covered in blood. They knew that the murderer of Caixi, seeing no way to escape, had hastily committed suicide by drowning. The murderer's body floated to the surface of the river at 10:00 AM and was pulled to the shore. The body was wearing a Western-style suit, a striped shirt, and a flannel vest. A murder weapon was found next to the body. There was a symbol on the clothing with the words "Zhong Zhenhu, platoon leader of the newly formed 54th Division." The Jiangning District Court was notified to conduct an autopsy. The details of the case are still under investigation. (15th Special Dispatch)

Chu Minyi Arrives in Beiping Yesterday

(Beiping) Chu Minyi arrived in Beiping this afternoon. He told reporters that he left Beiping hastily on the evening of the 29th of last month after performing "Dumukou." This time, the commander and deputy commander attended the National Assembly, truly able to achieve the eight characters of "consolidating unity and ensuring peace." I was urged by a letter from the French side to depart, so I requested leave from the National Assembly to come north, and also bid farewell to the representatives of the National Assembly, asking them to pay special attention to the development of the Northwest. I will go to Zhangjiakou in a day or two and take the "crawling car" directly to the Northwest. Zhang Xueliang will return north after the National Assembly closes. The central government and all parties advocate resolving the Guangdong issue politically and peacefully. The central government agreed to Hu Hanmin going abroad after the People's Conference. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will not come north for the time being. Li Shizeng will come to Beiping first after the Fifth Plenary Session. (15th Special Dispatch)

Luanzhou-Guangdong Stop Work Stoppage

General Labor Union Quietly Awaits Mediation

(Tianjin) Ding Zhanhai, a special commissioner sent by the province to mediate in Kailuan, returned to Tianjin from Tangshan on the 15th. He told reporters that the workers demanded a daily wage increase of two jiao, but the mining bureau did not approve it, and ordered a two-day shutdown each week. The workers' wage increase was unsuccessful, and they lost six yuan per month due to the shutdown, resulting in a work stoppage in five mines. After I arrived in Tangshan, I persuaded them to resume work and established a mediation committee. The mining bureau requested a meeting in Tianjin, and is currently seeking instructions from the provincial government regarding when to move to Tianjin for negotiations. It is also heard that since the mine was taken over by another person, the management has been poor, and there have been frequent incidents of workers being injured. There are currently over ninety injured workers in the hospital. (

15th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Kailuan General Labor Union telegraphed on the 15th, stating that it has accepted the advice of both the Party and government, stopped the work stoppage, and is quietly awaiting mediation. The regiment has reported the matter to the Garrison Headquarters for handling. (15th Special Dispatch)

Foreign Important Telegrams

Pan-European Preparatory Committee Holds First Meeting

Briand as Chairman

Discussing Routine Business

Italian Representative Will Have New Proposal

National News, Geneva, 15th: The Preparatory Committee of the European Federation first held informal talks with the representatives who had arrived yesterday, exchanging opinions. Today, the first meeting was held. French Foreign Minister Briand arrived here just a few hours ago and attended as chairman. The matters discussed were routine business, the report of the previous organizing committee, and inviting Danzig Free City to participate in the economic conference as in the case of Russia, Turkey, and Iceland. Therefore, the discussion was not public. At today's meeting, German Foreign Minister Curtius had lengthy talks with British Foreign Secretary Henderson, followed by Italian Foreign Secretary Grandi. However, the Soviet Russian representative will not arrive until late tonight, so the formal discussion of economic issues will be at the earliest tomorrow afternoon. National News, Geneva, 14th: Representatives from various countries have arrived successively. Among them, Italian Foreign Secretary Grandi is the most active. After meeting with British Foreign Secretary Henderson and Austrian Foreign Minister Schober, Grandi gave a speech to domestic journalists stationed in Geneva. In his speech, Grandi declared that Italy will present new proposals to various countries within the next few days, and that the new proposals have been endorsed by Henderson. It is understood that Grandi's new proposals are actually derived from the original proposal for a European customs union and customs truce, with the aim of stopping tariff increases. Grandi further stated that Italy believes that the only good way to achieve the goal of a European customs truce is for two or three neighboring countries to first unite, and then for small unions to form large unions, so that a great European union can be established. National News, Geneva, 14th: The German delegation arrived here at noon today. Foreign Minister Curtius visited Austrian Prime Minister Schober immediately after getting off the train and had lengthy discussions on the German-Austrian customs agreement.

Egyptian Parliamentary Primary Election Leads to Serious Riots

Authorities Adopt High-Pressure Tactics

Expected to Cause Changes in the Situation

Reuters, Cairo, 14th: Riots broke out in the industrial area of Cairo this morning. According to the relief society, a total of 18 people died, but officials said that 5 people died and 60 were injured. This riot is unprecedented in Cairo in recent years and was caused by the parliamentary primary election. Most of the rioters were striking workers who knocked down streetlights and engaged in other acts of destruction. Egyptian infantry was dispatched to suppress the riots, and the riots subsided. The scene has improved tonight, but troops are still patrolling the streets.

National News, Cairo, 15th: After yesterday's election turmoil, observers expect major changes in the Egyptian political situation soon. Both the Liberal Party and the Nationalist Party are boycotting the election. It is predicted that if the government wants to maintain its power, it will resort to extreme high-pressure tactics. Election tides are also occurring in many provinces at this time. For example, in Piyo Saif, a military-civilian conflict resulted in 4 deaths and 9 injuries. Therefore, the current situation must be considered extremely serious.

New Spanish Polity

Tending to Create a Republican Dictatorship

Deposed King Alfonso's Property Confiscated

National News, Madrid, 15th: The newly appointed Police Chief Garay Echeverría declared that he intends to recruit workers to organize republican militia and entrust them with the important task of safeguarding the republican system and curbing restoration. However, observers predict that after this plan is realized, Spain will see a period of republican dictatorship. Furthermore, many key figures in the Spanish intellectual class issued a declaration today opposing the expulsion of religious orders and asked the people of the whole country to maintain order and save the country from the chaos.

National News, Madrid, 14th: The Spanish government has issued an order to confiscate all property left in the country by the deposed King Alfonso, because he abused his royal position and increased his private wealth by illegal means. The former king secretly transported large amounts of money to foreign countries during the period when the export of capital was prohibited. At that time, in order to prevent the continued decline of the Spanish currency, anyone who secretly transported money abroad was severely punished. Currently, the former king has a deposit of 350,000 pounds in British banks, and deposits in France and other countries are not included. In addition, the royal treasures were secretly transported abroad in advance, and even famous paintings in the palace were taken away.

National News, Rome, 14th: The Pope's protest to the Spanish government has been delivered by the Pope's envoy to Spain. The wording is still peaceful, in order to avoid the severance of diplomatic relations.

US and Japan Pay Attention to the International Silver Conference Issue

Reuters, Washington, 14th: The movement to hold an international conference to discuss silver prices is gradually gaining momentum. Today's news is that if China has representatives attending, the United States can participate in the conference. The United States also suggested that such a conference should be held in a suitable location such as Geneva.

Reuters, Tokyo, 15th: For the purpose of gathering opinions on the international silver conference, the Japanese Minister of Finance convened a meeting of ministry officials and key figures in the Japanese business community this afternoon to discuss this issue. It is expected that most people will advocate temporarily taking a passive attitude and waiting for the United Kingdom, the United States, and other countries to express their attitudes. Another dispatch stated that the Minister of Finance has discussed the location of the silver conference proposed by the International Chamber of Commerce with key figures in the banking and business communities. A special committee has been established and will continue to discuss this matter tomorrow.

British Airship Policy Changes Financial Policy

Conservatives Propose Amendments

Reuters, London, 14th: British Prime Minister MacDonald stated in the House of Commons today that British airship policy and procedures must be completely changed after the R-101 accident. No more airships will be built, and the existing R-100 will be converted into a test airship, because there are various unresolved problems that still need to be studied. However, it will not be used for long-distance flights. The funding for maintaining and researching this ship will be 120,000 pounds in the first year, 130,000 pounds in the second and third years, and at most 140,000 pounds. After three or four years, a plan will be determined. If three years of research show the government that maintaining this ship is useless, it will be abandoned. If it is found that the future of airships is very promising, it will be expanded. Conservative Hoare said that airships may be very beneficial to the British Empire in the future, so the research and testing work that has been carried out for five years should not be terminated. Liberal Simon also supported the Prime Minister's proposal.

Reuters, London, 14th: The Conservative Party has proposed an amendment in the House of Commons, disagreeing with the Snowden budget bill scheduled for a second reading on May 19th. The most opposed is the proposal to levy land tax.

Russian Government's Plan to Develop North Pacific Fisheries

Decided to Fund the Construction of Far East Ports

Teletype, Tokyo, 15th: The branch of the transportation department of the Soviet Russian government's trade bureau received confirmation yesterday that the Soviet Russian side, in order to develop North Pacific fisheries, has decided to build large-scale shipyards in Vladivostok, Nikolaevsk-on-Amur, Aleksandrovsk, and other Far East ports. At the same time, it plans to open up new ports along the coastal areas of North Sakhalin and other areas, and greatly increase the number of merchant fleets. The funding has now been decided.

Public Telegrams

Telegram from the Hankou Party Headquarters Requesting Correction of Deng Gu et al.'s Erroneous Statements Addressed to all levels of Party Headquarters nationwide, Provincial and Municipal Governments, all Organizations, all Legal Entities, all Newspapers, and to be forwarded to all Compatriots for their information: The following is a telegram sent to the National Conference today: To the National Conference, for the perusal of the Nanjing Central Executive Committee: Since the auspicious opening of your esteemed assembly, good news has spread, and the whole country rejoices. The focus of the discussions these past ten days has been on consolidating peace and striving for construction. This is truly enough to console the spirit of the late Premier in Heaven and to live up to the hopes of the people for good governance, thereby solidifying our national foundation. We look up to you as our guide and are filled with admiration beyond description. Unexpectedly, at a time when the whole country is placing its hopes on you, Deng Zeru and others, who have fallen into disgrace, suddenly issued a circular telegram last month, picking up rumors and making erroneous accusations. All Chinese people are deeply shocked and puzzled. We later learned that Mr. Cai Zimin and other members of the Central Supervisory Committee had already sent a telegram to correct them, hoping that Deng Zeru and others would soon feel ashamed and repent. However, Cantonese generals Chen Jitang and others, oblivious to the greater good, again sent a Jiang telegram. The call for safeguarding peace and unity is at its height, but their inferior nature of fomenting chaos has resurfaced. This kind of behavior is not only forbidden by Party discipline and national law, but also intolerable to the public and reason. Moreover, the fierce flames of the Red bandits have not yet been quelled. Anyone with a conscience thinks of uniting as one to overcome the difficulties together. How can we allow madmen with lost hearts and minds to spread rumors and advocate chaos, willingly creating opportunities for the Red bandits? Thinking of this, we are filled with worry and indignation. Your esteemed assembly is a group representing the public will of the people, and you are deeply concerned about the national economy and the people's livelihood. Therefore, we respectfully request that you swiftly correct the erroneous statements in the telegram from Deng Zeru and others to maintain discipline and rectify public opinion. We await your orders with utmost anticipation. We sincerely hope that all compatriots and comrades of the Party will unite in advocating this. We remain, the Provisional Reorganization Committee of the Hankou Special Municipality Party Headquarters of the Chinese Kuomintang, respectfully, Yuan Yin.

Telegram from Anqing Addressed to all Newspapers for their perusal: We have just replied to Director He Jingzhi et al. with the following telegram: Upon reading your sincere telegram, we deeply admire your righteous and stern advice to the Cantonese Chen. We are currently following the teachings of the late Premier to realize the National Conference. The whole country, from top to bottom, should sincerely support and implement the resolutions. Internally, we should strictly abide by the provisional constitution and promote the progress of political tutelage. Externally, we should revise treaties and strive for international equality. How can we hold private opinions and rashly start disputes? Moreover, the people are tired of chaos and yearn for peace, and the Red calamity is rampant and urgently needs to be suppressed. We should not be used by others and willingly become leaders of bandits, plunging the Republic into danger and acting as pioneers for the Red bandits. If Bo Nan truly has the country at heart, he will be able to follow our sincere advice, repent and reform, eliminate discord, and establish harmony. Diao Yuan et al. are loyal to the Party and the country, and our duty is to defend, conquer, and quell the chaos. We will only follow the orders of the Central Government. If it benefits the country, we will not hesitate. We hope that the leaders of the Party and the government, our comrades in the army, and all compatriots nationwide will rise up together and work together to stop the source of chaos. It would be fortunate for the Party and the country. Chen Diaoyuan, Fan Xiji, Yue Shengxuan, Ruan Zhaochang, Liang Hongen, respectfully, Yuan.

Important News

National Government Bestows Medals of Honor Yesterday Morning

Seventeen Generals Received Medals

The National Government held a ceremony for awarding medals at 8:00 AM this morning (the 15th) in the Great Auditorium. Present were Chairman Jiang Zhongzheng, heads of various agencies He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Chen Guofu, Yang Shuzhuang, Liu Shangqing, He Yaozu, Chen Qicai, etc., and over two hundred staff and guests. After the ceremony was performed according to protocol, medals were awarded to the following generals: (1) Awarded the First Class Baoding Medal: Liu Zhi, Commander-in-Chief of the Second Army Corps; Han Fuqu, Commander-in-Chief of the First Army Corps; Xu Yuanquan, Commander-in-Chief of the Sixteenth Route Army; Wang Jun, Commander of the Third Military Region; (2) Awarded the Second Class Baoding Medal: He Jian, Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Route Army; Fang Benren, Director of the Beiping Pacification Headquarters (All generals receiving awards were in military uniform with swords, except for Fang, who wore a long gown with a National Conference badge); Ma Hongkui, Commander-in-Chief of the Fifteenth Route Army; Chen Cheng, Commander of the Eighteenth Army; Zhao Guantao, Commander of the Sixth Division; Lu Diping, Commander-in-Chief of the Ninth Route Army; Li Mingzhong, Superintendent of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Region Pacification; Jiang Bocheng, Chief Counselor of the Pacification Headquarters; Zhang Fang, Commander-in-Chief of the Twentieth Route Army; (3) Awarded the Third Class Baoding Medal: Dai Jun, Commander of the Tenth Division; Zhou Lun, Deputy Director of the General Staff Office of the Commander-in-Chief; (4) Awarded the Fourth Class Baoding Medal: Li Shiding, Chief of Staff of the Seventh Division; Zeng Wanzhong, Brigade Commander of the Seventh Division. After the awarding of the medals, Chairman Jiang gave a speech, roughly stating: "It is gratifying that all the officers and soldiers have been inspired by the late Premier's ideology over the years, united as one, and have brought the country to its current position. It is even more meaningful to award you medals during the National Conference. I hope you will always remember the late Premier's teachings to revolutionary soldiers, that you are pioneers for the people, working tirelessly day and night, following the ideology, being diligent and brave, faithful and loyal. You must also always remember the subordinates who have been inspired by the ideology and sacrificed for the revolution under your command. You must know that our success is entirely due to the power of the ideology. We as individuals have no merit of our own. After receiving these medals today, I hope you will work harder, continue your past spirit, and strive for the country's construction and unification, so that the achievements of the revolution will be preserved forever and remain immortal." After the speech, the ceremony concluded and the attendees dispersed.

Recent Financial Situation in Guangdong Province

Tax Revenue Collected in Cash Starting in May

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the Central Bank suspended convertibility in Guangdong Province, the market price of banknotes is currently about 80% of cash. The daily opening prices for buying and selling at silver shops also fluctuate between 79% and 80%. Yang Jianping, the Deputy Governor of the Central Bank, has resigned, and Huang Guanzhang has been sent by the head office to replace him. However, since the Central Bank suspended convertibility, its branches in various regions have also announced suspension of convertibility. Therefore, the Central Bank's business has been very quiet recently. It is rumored that the bank still has more than one million yuan in funds. Fan Qiwu, the Director of the Finance Department, has resigned and is temporarily replaced by Lin Yungai, a member of the Provincial Committee. Lin took over affairs at the Finance Department on the 11th. Starting on May 1st, tax revenues in Guangdong Province have been converted to collection in silver coins, according to the following methods for revenue and expenditure: (A) Revenue: (1) Starting on May 1st, all tax revenues in the province that were originally collected in Central Bank banknotes will be collected in full cash. The four prefectures of Chaozhou, Meizhou, Qinzhou, and Lianzhou, which previously collected land name bonds, will continue to collect land name bonds without any changes. However, if the land name bonds have been announced to be non-convertible, they will also be collected in full cash. (2) Before May 1st (i.e., up to the end of April), the Central Bank banknotes collected by various counties and authorized collection agencies should be verified by May 15th. The amounts, along with the revenue statements and receipt stubs, should be reported for verification and then deposited into the treasury. Failure to do so will result in a penalty of silver coins. The amount of funds contracted by the merchants and companies that are based on silver coins should be collected in cash, whether it is salary owed before the end of April or new salary after May. They should not use Central Bank banknotes to settle the debt. (B) Expenditure: (1) The expenses of various agencies, whether regular, temporary, or commission fees, will be paid in full cash starting on May 1st. For expenses incurred before April, except for military expenses and those specifically approved to be paid in silver coins, whether payment orders have been issued or not, will be paid in Central Bank banknotes. (2) The four prefectures of Chaozhou, Meizhou, Qinzhou, and Lianzhou, which previously paid with land name bonds, will continue to pay as before without any changes. However, if the land name bonds have been announced to be non-convertible, the first method should still be applied. (3) The principal and interest of financial treasury bonds will continue to be paid with Central Bank banknotes starting on May 1st. The remaining silver coins will be used to consolidate the Central Bank's funds. (May 12th)

Jiaoji Railway Decides to Extend the Route

Extending Westward from Jinan

Surveyed in Eight Lines

Qingdao Correspondence: The Jiaoji Railway Bureau previously considered that the entire line was only over 400 kilometers long, limiting the absorption of merchants and goods to the eastern part of Shandong Province. Inter-station transportation was limited to the Jinpu line. In order to make full use of the superior location of Qingdao Port, develop railway business, and increase passenger and freight revenue, it was proposed to extend the existing line westward from Jinan, so that it would be close to the Grand Canal and further connect with the Pinghan line. This would allow all goods from north and south of the Yellow River and east and west of the Grand Canal to be directly exported through the Jiaoji Railway, benefiting the sale of local products and increasing the railway's economy. The first line would extend from Jinan to Linqing. The Engineering Department organized a survey team to conduct on-site surveys and detailed investigations into the economic conditions along the line. At the same time, three lines from Linqing to Shunde, Zhangde, or Daokou were also planned for preliminary surveys and economic investigations, so that routes could be selected when extending the line in the future. It is now learned that the railway has formulated a plan for surveying the extended route, which has been divided into two types: exploration and preliminary survey. The exploration will be conducted on eight lines: Jinan to Dongchang, Jinan to Linqing, Linqing to Shunde, Linqing to Zhangde, Linqing to Daokou, Dongchang to Linqing, Dongchang to Zhangde, and Dongchang to Daokou. Preliminary surveys will also be conducted on the two lines from Jinan to Dongchang and Jinan to Linqing. The plan has been submitted to the Ministry of Railways and approved. (May 12th)

A Batch of Books from the Haiyuan Pavilion Discovered

A Total of Twenty Titles, Mostly Rare Song and Yuan Editions

Liu Songnian is Willing to Sell to the Library

Jinan Correspondence: The loss of books from the Haiyuan Pavilion of the Yang family in Liaocheng has been reported in previous letters. Recently, a batch of books from the Haiyuan Pavilion was discovered in the Jinan market. It turns out that when Wang Guanjun's troops looted books from the Haiyuan Pavilion last year and headed north, they passed through Gaotang. One soldier, finding several sacks of books cumbersome, sold them to Liu Songnian, the director of the Gaotang Post Office, for sixty strings of cash (equivalent to three thousand copper coins). Liu did not pay much attention to the books at first. He entrusted a friend to sell them in Jinan, saying that if they were sold to the library for the public benefit, he would accept a lower price, as Liu is a public-spirited person. His friend came to Jinan and told Wang Xiantang, the director of the Provincial Library. Wang, knowing that they were books from the Haiyuan Pavilion, asked him to negotiate with Liu Songnian. The books have now been transported to Jinan, totaling twenty titles, mostly rare Song and Yuan editions, but some are incomplete. They include: (1) Yuan edition of Zhu Wen Gong's Commentary on Han Changli's Writings (complete), the main collection in forty volumes, the outer collection in blank volumes, and a volume of collected anecdotes and poems. (2) Fugubian (complete), Qing edition. (3) Manuscript of the Fengyunlou Book List (complete), Wang blank Sun's collection. (4) Manuscript of the Qinghuatang Poetry Draft (complete). (5) Manuscript of Mr. Xiong Wuxuan's Writings (complete). (6) Chunqiu Guliang Zhuan. (7) Dam Ming Yitong Zhi (incomplete), Ming edition. (8) Dongxiyang Kao (complete), Ming edition. (9) Du Gongbu (complete), Ming edition. (10) Manuscript of the Jiaoming Ji (complete). (11) Yuan edition of the Fan Deji Collection (complete). (12) Manuscript of the Wang Shuiyun Collection (complete). (13) Ming edition of the Ji Zhongsan Collection (complete). (14) Manuscript of the Shulin Waiji (complete). (15) Kaicheng Stone Classics (incomplete). (16) Manuscript of the Beitang Shuchao (incomplete). (17) Song edition of the Wei Suzhou Collection (one volume missing). (18) Liuyi Wenchao (complete). (19) Hailu Suishi (incomplete). (20) Hu-engraved Zizhi Tongjian (incomplete). After examining the books, Wang Xiantang directly wrote to Liu Songnian to negotiate. The main points of the original letter were: "I heard that you intend to sell all the books from the Haiyuan Pavilion to our library, and your public spirit is admirable. The estimated current market value of the books is eight hundred yuan, but if you sell them to booksellers, the price would be less. Our library is currently in contact with Yang Jingfu, the owner of the Haiyuan Pavilion, to have him donate half and sell half of his entire collection to the library, requesting the National Government to commend Mr. Yang. It would be best if you also sold the books at half price (four hundred yuan) to the library. Please also fulfill this kindness and ask the ministry to commend you with the Shandong Postal Administration." Liu Songnian is quite enlightened, and it is likely that this matter will be successful. The library has also recently purchased a copy of Xue's Inscriptions on Bells and Tripods, a manuscript from the Haiyuan Pavilion collection, for thirty yuan (incomplete). The book is finely copied on gold-flecked scripture paper from Mount Jinsu. The Haiyuan Pavilion Book List engraved by Jiang Jianxia originally had two volumes, but only one remains. The Qilu University Library in the city has also purchased two kinds of books from the Haiyuan Pavilion collection, but the titles are not detailed. (May 13th)

Communist Bandits Massacre in Ruijin

Many Bandits Killed in Suichuan and Anfu

Nanchang Correspondence: The bandits on the east bank of the Gan River, due to being severely suppressed by the National Army, are moving in large numbers to the east of Gan and Fujian. It is reported by refugees fleeing Ruijin that the county has been brutally massacred by bandits for many years, with about tens of thousands of people killed and over twenty million yuan in property lost. Fortunately, the local customs are strong, and a militia has been formed to resist the bandits, preventing them from being completely slaughtered by the Red bandits. Last winter, the local militia joined forces to recover the county seat, gaining some peace. Unexpectedly, this spring, Deng Yi's troops of the Red Army's pseudo-35th Army infiltrated Ruijin from Yunmenling and carried out a major massacre. Luo Binghui's troops of the pseudo-12th Army then joined Deng's troops from Ningdu to attack the county seat. The militia, outnumbered, lost the county seat again. After the bandits entered the city, the county government, the Party headquarters, various public buildings, and slightly better houses were all burned to the ground. Jiubao, Gaoweinao, and other places, which were the concentration areas of the county's militia, were also captured. Residents, young and old, fled. Because the Luo blank bandits blank the local residents blank blank, people were killed indiscriminately. Blank members of the Nine blank People blank blank and Tong Rongdi blank and hundreds of others were killed. Hundreds of buildings in Yangjiaze were blank blank. Hundreds of people, including Yang Jiaqiu, were captured, extorted, and imprisoned in the bandits' lair. Tens of thousands of farmers from the surrounding villages blank fled to Ganzhou, and thousands more fled to Huichang Yunmenling, all displaced, in a state of wanting to live but being unable to die. It is indeed tragic. Suichuan was previously occupied by Li Mingrui's troops. After being recovered by Luo Lin's division, it was guarded by the county police force. On the 28th of last month, a large number of Red bandits suddenly rushed into the county seat. County Magistrate Wang and the police force, caught off guard, withdrew from the city and gathered their troops to fight back with all their might, causing the bandits to retreat from the county seat. Some Red bandits, unable to retreat in time, were disarmed by the police force. As for Li Mingrui himself, at the end of last month, he led the pseudo-7th Army from Yongxin Suichuan to Anfu, launching a fierce attack on Anfu County. At that time, only one regiment of Han's division was in the city, and they defended the city to the death. The bandits used ladders to climb the city walls but were still repelled, with many bandits killed. Unable to succeed, the bandits retreated to Liaotangqiao, 25 li from the city, that night, intending to counterattack. The next day, government troops arrived to reinforce them, and the bandits were repelled again, with over two thousand bandits killed. The bandits then retreated to the Jinqingtian and Daonanzhen areas. Division Commander Han and Brigade Commander Zhang have now stationed their troops in the county to command their units and the police forces of Yongxin and Lianhua counties, joining forces with the Fourth Route Army to eliminate Li's bandits. (13th)

Pseudo-Communist Suppression Team Leader Arrested in Bengbu

Yan Weiyu Set Up a Scam to Defraud Money

Bengbu Correspondence: Yan Weiyu, who previously impersonated the commander of the Longjin Railway Communist Suppression Volunteer Team, falsely claimed to be under the direct jurisdiction of the central government in January of this year and led his accomplices in the areas of Xu, Bengbu and Linhuai. The Ji Battalion of the 268th Regiment of the 45th Division captured more than twenty of them in Linhuai. Division Commander Wei Lihuang telegraphed a report to the capital. The central government immediately issued an order to the garrison troops of Jiangsu, Anhui, Shandong, Henan and other provinces to cooperate in the arrest. Before long, Yan secretly came to Bengbu and hid behind the old Governor's Office on Erma Road. In recent months, Yan has falsely used the names of Zhang Fuyun, the Director of the National Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance, Zhang Gongchen of Anhui, and Yue Shengxuan, the Commander of the 46th Division, to forge appointment letters from the Anhui Provincial Tobacco Prohibition Bureau and the Anhui Provincial Tobacco Prohibition Committee, and privately engraved seals and sold official positions such as District Director, Deputy Director, Branch Director, and Inspector, charging dozens to hundreds of yuan per position. Miao Jiesan of Suxian County, desiring to obtain a position as Director of a Tobacco Prohibition Branch Bureau, gave Yan 800 yuan, plus miscellaneous expenses, totaling more than 1,000 yuan. Yan then gave Miao a fake appointment letter. However, Miao has not been able to take office from March to now. Miao realized that he had been deceived by Yan, and was very angry. A few days ago, he submitted a document to the Northern Anhui Garrison Headquarters accusing Yan of fraud and requesting his arrest and investigation. At the same time, Liu Yisan, the former confidential secretary of the pseudo-Communist Suppression Volunteer Team, also filed a complaint, saying that Yan had swindled him out of five box cannons last year. These guns were borrowed from someone, and Yan had repeatedly refused to return them. He also accused Yan of extorting more than 1,000 yuan from someone named Jia in Renqiao, and requested his prompt arrest and investigation to recover the guns. Upon receiving the report, the Garrison Headquarters dispatched a team at noon on the 12th to arrest Yan Weiyu at his address and seized many pieces of evidence. He was sent to the Public Security Bureau that night for detention. Yesterday (the 13th) afternoon, the Garrison Headquarters sent a team to bring Yan back for interrogation by the Military Law Office. Yan suddenly claimed to be ill and was temporarily released on bail to a hospital for treatment. He will be summoned for interrogation as soon as he recovers. (14th)

Northern Wei Antiquities from Tianlong Mountain

Occupying an Extremely Important Position in Art

There are Rumors of Theft and Sale

Taiyuan Correspondence: Tianlong Mountain in Taiyuan County, Shanxi Province, is a famous scenic spot. There is a temple at the foot of the mountain, about eighty li from the provincial capital. Cars can reach the vicinity. The temple buildings are magnificent, and the trees reach the sky, making it look like a large village. The four mountains surround it, with cliffs standing upright. There are ancient cypresses on the top of the mountain that are more than a dozen feet in circumference. However, due to the rugged mountain roads, many tourists have not been able to get a close look. The scenery is excellent, and the terrain is relatively high, and the climate is very cool. In recent years, many Chinese and foreigners have gone there to escape the summer heat. The mountain walls have Buddhist statues made during the Northern Wei Dynasty, carved into recessed shapes in the stone walls. They are a masterpiece of the Northern Wei Tuoba clan during its heyday, occupying an extremely important position in Eastern art and sculpture history. According to art critics, their value is higher than that of the Yungang Grottoes in Datong. Therefore, they are highly admired by Chinese and foreigners, especially the Japanese. Since Dr. Tokiwa Daijo, a Japanese literary scholar, published a masterpiece describing their value, they have attracted the attention of scholars in the East and West. In the 15th year of the Republic of China, the Crown Prince of Sweden came to Shanxi to investigate and regarded them as national treasures of China. The number of Japanese who come to Shanxi every year specifically to visit this mountain is even more numerous. Even a brick or a piece of wood is considered a treasure, so many people pick up broken tiles from the temple. A student from a certain Japanese university, using the art of the temple as material for his doctoral dissertation, has come to Shanxi. Due to its reputation, unscrupulous people always want to steal and sell them to obtain huge sums of money. There have been repeated thefts in the past two or three years, which have caused a national sensation. In order to preserve the national essence, the Ministry of Education telegraphed the Shanxi Provincial Government last spring, requesting that it be carefully protected. The Provincial Government immediately ordered Taiyuan County to investigate. The Magistrate of Taiyuan County then expelled the abbot of the temple and sent a special commissioner to guard it. It is now learned that a man named Wang Shanting, a native of Hebei, who was previously a section chief of the Tianjin Executive Headquarters of the Pingjin Garrison Command, came to Shanxi in desperation and bribed the guards of Tianlong Mountain, blank precious statues, blank blank, the situation blank blank people, still higher than Bing blank, I do not know why the authorities of Shanxi province do not strictly investigate this matter, (10th)

Hangzhou Express Mail

Zhejiang's sericulture is the best in the country. Most of the silk firms in the eastern and western counties of Zhejiang have closed down due to financial reasons. Farmers in the countryside have already finished raising silkworms and the cocoons have already been harvested. The silk firms in Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou have opened for business one after another since the 16th. It is reported that the silkworm production is not as good as last year, and the price of cocoons at the silk firms is about 46 yuan per hundred catties.

The Hangzhou Silk Weaving Industry Association has initiated the organization of a cooperative to specialize in large quantities of rayon and distribute it to various industries. It has been decided to raise 50,000 yuan through the subscription of shares by members of the association. The subscription of shares has been very enthusiastic, and more than half of the funds have already been paid. The members of the cooperative have been selected and assigned to work. All rayon required by the weaving households will be issued by the cooperative at cost price to the entire industry, which will reduce expenses by more than 5,000 yuan per month.

The tenth round of principal repayment lottery for old debt bonds in Zhejiang Province will be held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce today (the 15th) at 3:00 PM. The bonds are divided into ten groups, and one ticket will be drawn from each group to be the winning ticket. Regardless of whether the bond is for five, ten, one hundred, or one thousand yuan, if the last two characters of the bond match the winning number, the principal will be repaid according to the face value of the bond. The winning numbers are 03, 13, 24, 30, 43, 59, 68, 78, 90, and 96. The total amount of principal to be repaid this time is 369,000 yuan, and the interest is 5400 yuan. It has been decided that starting from June 1st, the principal and interest will be repaid by the local banks of China and the county governments upon presentation of the bond and verification of the winning number.

The Zhejiang Provincial Clearing-up-the-Countryside campaign will be conducted in three phases (one month per phase). The Clearing-up-the-Countryside General Bureau yesterday issued an order to the branch bureaus in each county and city to comply. The Hangzhou County Clearing-up-the-Countryside Bureau has decided to implement the investigation starting on the 26th, with the district chiefs and police stations responsible for handling it. (15th)

Verdict in the Case of Mother-in-Law and Daughter-in-Law Arguing Over Support: The case of Xu Ding, a young woman from Shanghai, demanding 10,000 yuan in alimony from her father-in-law, Xu Zhilan, has been won in the Shanghai District Court. Xu Zhilan, dissatisfied with the verdict, appealed to the High Court. The case was concluded on the 12th of this month by Shen Yuan, the presiding judge of the First Civil Division of the High Court. The verdict was announced at 2:00 PM yesterday (the 15th). The original verdict was that Xu Zhilan's lawsuit against Xu Ding was dismissed, except for the rejection of the appellant's remaining claims and the application for provisional execution. The appellant's lawsuit regarding alimony in the first instance and the incidental appeal were both dismissed. The costs of the case are to be borne by the appellant.
