Afterwards, the 13th Water Police Team stationed in Changshu arrested Luo Zengquan, Jin Changxi, and Chen Changcai, three people from Taicang County, outside the West Gate. According to their statements, they had legitimate occupations, and they were released on bail on the 13th. However, on the afternoon of the 12th, the team received a tip that the robbers were hiding in Dahu Dian outside the South Gate. Upon receiving the report, Team Leader Yang Qingjiu dispatched Officer Hu to Dahu Dian with the informant on the morning of the 13th, where they arrested Chen Er and Wu Da. Later, they captured a bandit ship in front of the Daxing Warehouse in Yongjiqiao, and arrested Wang Xiaolao Han and Jiang Xiaoliuzi, two people, on the ship. They were all taken to the Second Platoon and transferred to the 13th Team Headquarters. After Team Leader Yang personally interrogated them, Chen Er confessed that his other name was Jinbao, a native of Yancheng. On the eighth day of the third month of the lunar calendar, he and Wu Da, Wang Xiaolao Han, and others sailed to the Huqiao area outside the West Gate, planning to land there to steal chickens. Unexpectedly, in the middle of the night, a merchant boat passed by, and they had the idea of robbing it. They robbed the boat and took 84 pieces of cloth, 20 yuan in foreign currency, and more than 20,000 copper coins. There was nothing else. The cloth had already been pawned, and the money had been spent. When questioned, Jiang Xiaoliuzi only claimed that he was sailing the boat for them and denied any robbery. The statements of Wu Da and Wang Xiaolao Han were similar to Chen Er's. Based on the confessions, Team Leader Yang temporarily detained the bandits at the team headquarters and decided to hand them over to the Suzhou District Headquarters for interrogation on the 14th.

Jiangyin

Zhanwenqiao Defense Corps Captures Bandits: At about 2 PM on the 14th, several bandits suddenly came to rob the home of villager Chen A-mo in Chenjiagang, 7 li from Zhanwenqiao Street, Second District of Dongwai. Because only women were at home, the bandits set a fire. The Zhanwenqiao Defense Corps heard the alarm and went to the scene, capturing one bandit, wounding one corps member, and burning two bandits to death. The captured bandit was handed over to the county for processing.

The Truth About Sub-Bureau Chief's Private Torture of Chen Xianghan: Huang Zhifang, the sub-bureau chief of the Houmu Public Security Third Sub-bureau, in order to prevent merchants from celebrating the opening of the National Assembly, prohibited theatrical performances, causing a market strike. He arbitrarily arrested Chen Xianghan and privately tortured him. Zhou Fanshun, a patrol officer, advised him to stop, but Huang Zhifang did not listen. Later, because Ren Shaoshan stood up for Chen Xianghan to the merchants, proving that Chen Xianghan had indeed been privately tortured, Huang Zhifang used the excuse of inciting a market strike to arrest Ren Shaoshan and send him to the county for interrogation. The merchants of Houmu strongly refuted this, saying that Huang Zhifang's private torture of Chen Xianghan caused serious injuries, and there were injury reports and witnesses. But Ren Shaoshan was groundlessly arrested and sent to the county for interrogation. Chen Xianghan left the sub-bureau, and Sub-bureau Chief Huang set off firecrackers late at night and respectfully escorted him home before the market was allowed to open.

Jiang Sheng Daily is Sued: Wu Jiangshi, the widow of the late shop owner Wu Yufeng of the Wu Yisheng Rice Shop in Jintongqiao, First District, hired lawyer Xia Ding because the Jiang Sheng Daily published a news item on April 17 about plotting to seize his wife's property, which damaged his reputation. He filed a criminal lawsuit with the county government. Yesterday (the 13th) afternoon, Judge Wu heard the case in court. The plaintiff Wu Jiangshi and the editor of the Jiang Sheng Daily, Wang Sengru, were present. The judge asked the plaintiff which newspaper was being sued. The plaintiff did not know how to answer, only saying it was a newspaper. She then said that because the news had damaged his reputation, he had asked his maternal uncle, Zhang Liangshi, to write a letter to the newspaper on the 18th to make a correction, but it was not published, so he filed the lawsuit. When questioned, Wang Sengru said that the news item was a submitted manuscript, and it was difficult to judge whether it was true or not. However, if there was a mistake, he could send a letter to make a correction according to the publishing law, but the newspaper had not received a letter from Wu Jiangshi. Wu Jiangshi's lawsuit did not mention that the lawsuit was filed because no correction was made. After the hearing, the judge ordered Zhang Liangshi to be summoned to court for further investigation.

Yangzhou

Bandits Arrested in Yizheng and Sent to the Governor's Office for Interrogation: The Pacification Governor's Office previously received a report from a farmer named Peng in Guishan Village, Yizheng, stating that a seven-and-a-half-month-old child had been abducted by bandits and torn up. The Yizheng County was ordered to investigate and bring the perpetrators to justice. Shi Maozhong, Peng Dezhao, Peng Guangshan, Chen Dingfu, Zhou Kuaizi, Xiao Shenqi, and Chen Pengshi, seven people in total, have now been arrested by the county. They were escorted to the office this morning to await trial.

Nantong

Four Representatives Go to Beijing to Petition: The 11th Division of Hankou sent personnel to Nantong to prepare for the establishment of a disabled soldiers' vocational training factory, which was unanimously opposed by all sectors of society. On the 13th, Zhao Jian and three others were selected to go to Beijing to petition the headquarters. Various organizations and the Chinese Association telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Chiang, saying, "We, the association, etc., believe that the 11th Division stationed in Hankou designated to establish a disabled soldiers' factory in Nantong has many obstacles. We submitted it to the party and government organs and held a joint meeting. Zhao Jianhua, Cheng Yunke, Hou Ruzhou, and Wang Jimin were publicly elected as petition representatives. We respectfully submit the reasons why a disabled soldiers' factory cannot be established in Nantong. We respectfully request that Your Excellency grant an audience and promptly order the division to select another location, etc." Zhuang Mingyuan, a member of the 11th Division Committee, returned to Hankou on the 13th to ask for instructions due to local opposition.

Robberies and Assaults Occur Frequently in Urban and Rural Areas: The atmosphere in the urban and rural areas of Nantong is uneasy. At 2 a.m. on the 14th, the Lu family east of Hongmiao was robbed, and the victim was killed. The Gaolian Nunnery was robbed, and the nuns were raped. Furthermore, an American named Xie Lesi was robbed by bandits near Houting in the west of the city. He has filed a complaint with the American consul for intervention. The county government, due to the frequent occurrence of banditry, has ordered the Public Security Bureau and the county police to patrol the roads from time to time. Because the census has been completed, a notice was issued to the people on the 14th, forbidding them to accommodate idlers. The Public Security Bureau was also ordered to investigate.

Change of Head of Shigang Anti-Smuggling Team: The head of the Shigang Huainan Salt Affairs Anti-Smuggling Water Team has been changed by the Anti-Smuggling Bureau to Ni Chong.

Huzhou

Kidnapping Occurs in Yaotou Village: In Yaotou Village, located at the border of Xiaang Town and Jingshan in Wuxing County, where there are more than 40 households, mostly surnamed Shen, two bandit ships suddenly arrived around 6 p.m. on the 10th of this month. About 20 bandits, each carrying firearms, rushed ashore and carried out a large-scale robbery in the village. Shen A-jin, Shen A-si, Shen A-xue, Shen Jitang and other four families were robbed, suffering huge losses. Six villagers, men and women, including Shen A-lian, Shen Xin-yuan, Shen A-jin, Shen A-mao, and Mao Mao, were kidnapped. After the incident, various authorities, upon hearing the news, dispatched police officers to investigate in all directions, but there was no trace of the bandits.

Pinghu

The Truth About Wang Jingqing's Appeal: Wang Jingqing of Ganhe Street in this city was sentenced to life imprisonment for attempted rape of Gai Zhao, which led to the woman's suicide out of shame and anger. Wang refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the High Court. According to reliable sources in Hangzhou, the High Court considered the appellant's appeal unreasonable and rejected it in court, dismissing the prosecution. The original sentence was still enforced. The rumors that he was resentenced to death by hanging in recent days were all false.

The Crisis of Education in Zha District: The educational funding in Zha District has always been extremely tight. In addition, the management committee has been mismanaging affairs, and the funding owed to various schools has been overdue for more than four months. The teachers and staff of various schools have been asking the principals for their salaries, and the principals have found it difficult to cope and unable to maintain operations. They will soon convene a meeting to unanimously petition the Education Bureau.

Hangzhou

Ancient Tomb of Concubine Song Wang Robbed: There is an ancient tomb of a Song Dynasty royal concubine in He Yan, Sanjiadun East Jiangqiao, Hangzhou County. Due to years of neglect, all the tomb stones have been stolen and sold by local ruffians. However, the concubine's coffin has not yet been excavated. Recently, a local tyrant named Zhu Xiaolei secretly colluded with unscrupulous people such as Jiang Tianfu, falsely claiming to be the landlord, and sold the tomb to Zhu. Zhu then hired workers to excavate it. Two ancient bottles and 7,000 ancient coins were found. A gap was also exposed in the soil, and a stone was thrown down, making a clanging sound, indicating that it was the place where the concubine's coffin was suspended. Originally, they intended to continue digging deeper to steal the treasures in the coffin, but because they were afraid of being seen, they covered it with soil again. A few days later, they summoned dozens of workers and built a mud wall around the tomb, which is now half completed. After it is completed, they plan to close the door and directly explore the location of the concubine's coffin and inspect the treasures inside. Local citizens Jiang Yifei, Xie Naichang, etc., believe that all antiquities should be preserved according to the law, and local people should not privately occupy or destroy them. Now that Zhu Xiaolei has illegally excavated the tomb of a famous concubine, he should be stopped. They specially wrote a letter to the provincial government requesting that officials be sent to investigate thoroughly and that Zhu Xiaolei and Jiang Tianfu be detained and brought to justice according to the law. After receiving the report, the provincial government ordered the Hangzhou County magistrate to investigate and report back for verification.

Shaoxing

Unbearable Wife-Murder Case: An unbearable wife-murder case occurred in Huangniutang, south of Shaoxing, yesterday. Yin Dachun, who works as a grocery store clerk in Heilongjiang, returns home once a year. His wife, Yin Zhao, is 31 years old and has two sons. Yin returned home in early May and heard that his wife had an affair, and they had an argument. Later, the wife's mother mediated, and they reconciled. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 10th, the woman suddenly shouted loudly. Neighbors heard the sound and went to check, but the husband had already fled. The woman was lying face down and unable to move. When people asked her the reason, she said that her husband had forced her to lie face down after intercourse, and then suddenly used a round wooden stick to stuff her vagina, causing serious injuries. She died tragically at midnight the next day. Her aunt prepared the body for burial. The incident was reported to the Lizhu Public Security Bureau, which reported it to the local branch court. Prosecutor Yang, accompanied by coroner Hu, went to the countryside to open the coffin for an autopsy. It was found that the vagina and uterus were broken, and the death was indeed caused by serious injuries sustained during her lifetime. The murderer is now being strictly apprehended and brought to justice for interrogation.

Ningbo

Compilation of Kidnapping Cases: Ma Mingluo, a resident of Majia Village, Yuntan Township, Yuyao, is from a family of modest means. The other night, more than ten bandits suddenly came and carried out a large-scale robbery, and kidnapped Ma Mingluo. At the same time, six or seven bandits went to the home of Ma Mingbao in the same place and carried out a robbery, also kidnapping Mingbao. Furthermore, in Zhangai Village, Meixu, Yin County, five or six bandits suddenly came to the home of resident Shen Xianghua the other day, and robbed gold jewelry, clothing, etc., worth about 400 yuan, and also stabbed the victim Shen Xianghua. Furthermore, two families, Wu Yongming and Zhang Liushi, in Baozhuang, Yin County, were robbed by bandits the other day of more than 200 yuan worth of clothing, gold jewelry, etc., and Wu Lushi and Wu Caiying were injured. Furthermore, more than ten bandits also came to the home of Zhou Lianzhong, a farmer in Suqiao near Xiwu, Fenghua, the other night. They entered through the front door. Zhou heard the alarm and secretly opened the back door to escape and sound the alarm. Neighbors gathered, and the bandits knew that things were not going well and fled in all directions. However, Zhou's house was surrounded by small rivers, making it difficult for the bandits to escape. Wang Shaoxi and Wang A-fu were arrested in the rice paddy and sent to the Clearing and Suppression Bureau for investigation. Furthermore, the family of Fan in Xiyu Village, Yuanyuan District, Fenghua, also had a few bandits who kidnapped his eight-year-old son yesterday, and his whereabouts are still unknown.

Dispute Over Gambling Leads to Murder: The Xinjian Tianlun arrived in Ningbo from Shanghai on the 12th. That evening, around 8 p.m., Jiang A-mao, a carpenter on the ship, and Zhang Yifa, a teahouse worker, had a dispute over gambling and fought each other. Unexpectedly, after the fight, Jiang A-mao returned to his room to sleep and suddenly felt severe pain in his chest. He immediately became unconscious and died shortly after. The incident was heard by the ship's purser, who, believing that Zhang Yifa had beaten Jiang, ordered the ship's police to watch Zhang. The next morning, the ship arrived at Ningbo port and reported the incident to the court for an autopsy. The suspect Zhang Yifa was taken to the court and sent to prison to await interrogation. Jiang's body is still displayed in the Zhaoshangju Alley, covered with a shed for safekeeping, pending resolution.

Education News and Sports

The First Day of the 5th Jiangnan University Games

——Field Event Championship…Central Taking the Lead…Jinan Will Strive

——Track Event Championship…Jinan is Promising…Central Must Work Hard

——Women's Championship…Central Women…Nineteen Have Confidence

—Zhonggong Ma Fengrui Sets New Meeting Record in 1500 Meters—

The 5th Jiangnan Eight University Joint Games, which started at 1:30 p.m. yesterday, was held at the new track and field stadium of Guanghua University on Daxilu Road. The sun was shining brightly, but unfortunately, the south wind was blowing wildly, making the competition very difficult. Central University has the advantage in field events, but Jinan will strive. In track events, Zhonggong Ma Fengrui set a new meeting record. The women's championship will not be a problem for Central women. The awards ceremony will be held at 5:00 p.m. today, and the closing ceremony will follow. The situation yesterday is described as follows:

Opening in the Wind

At 1:30 p.m., the meeting opened on time. At that time, the wind was raging, and very few athletes went to the podium. Chairman Wang Fudan performed the ceremony as usual. Honorary President Zhang Shouyong, President of Guanghua University, delivered a speech, saying that a strong country must first have a strong body, and sports is the key to strengthening the body. However, sports competitions must have victories and defeats. Victory is of course worth celebrating, and defeat should also be accepted with joy. Guanghua welcomes athletes from various schools to come to the school to hold the meeting, etc. Then, President Shi of the General Assembly gave a speech, and then the competition began.

Standing Committee Meeting

Yesterday morning, Wang Fudan, Shen Guoquan, and Zhang Changchang, members of the Track and Field Standing Committee of the Jiangnan Sports Association, held a meeting at Guanghua and decided that the women's relay race in this session would not be counted for points, and that each woman would be allowed to participate in four events. Other important cases were not discussed.

Final Details

1500 meters The men's track race yesterday only had this one final. Zhang Yuansheng of Central and Ma Fengrui of Zhonggong were the most promising, but Zhang had suffered from neurasthenia a few days ago. Yesterday, he failed to show his skills. Ma Fengrui led the way and no one could compete with him, winning first place with a new meeting record of 4 minutes 43 seconds 54. Zhou Mingzhang of Central was about 30 meters behind. It is said that Zhang Yuansheng had pushed Zhou back 40 to 50 meters at the Central University Games. Therefore, if Zhang was in good health yesterday, he would have been able to compete with Ma for first place, and the results would have been even more impressive.

Women's 200 meters Yesterday was originally a preliminary round, but it was changed to a final due to the small number of people. Huang Luanjiao of Jinan once led, with large steps and beautiful posture, but when there were 50 meters left, Wu Zhuhuan of Central suddenly sprinted and surpassed Ms. Luanjiao, winning the championship with a mediocre time of 33.8 seconds.

Men's High Jump The results of this event were not outstanding. Li Lin of Fudan failed at 1.60 meters, which was a pity. There were still five people at 1.63 meters. Wu Jinqi took the lead with 1.69 meters, and Chen Sui was second with 1.64 meters because he had just finished the high hurdles. The remaining three people all retreated to below 1.63 meters when determining the rankings, perhaps because they were all too nervous.

Women's High Jump There were only five participants at the beginning, and more came later. Ye Zhanmei of Central and Lu Weikun of Daxia competed fiercely, with the height difference being only one notch. Ye's result was a mediocre 1.18 meters. Women's Shot Put Wang Lan'yin of Jinan won first place with 7.98 meters. The athletes did not seem to be able to use their elasticity, so the throws were not far.

Men's Long Jump The most talented athletes were in the long jump. Zhao Rugong of Central, who was the most promising, committed two fouls and gave up on the third attempt, which was a pity. Wang Jihuai competed with illness and came from behind to win first place with 6.62 meters.

Men's Discus Throw The wind was very strong yesterday, and the results could not be improved. Wang Jihuai did not score points due to illness. Gao Shangzhi of Central won the championship with 31.0 meters, which was mediocre.

Wang Jihuai, the King of Field Events from Guanghua, ate several packs of ice cream the day before, followed by noodles, and then ate ice cream again, resulting in severe diarrhea. He competed with illness yesterday, so he did not score in the discus throw, but he still won first place in the long jump.

Championship Situation

—Central and Jinan—

—Already Engaged in Close Combat—

In this year's conference, Central University, with the status of last year's champion, arrived with a large contingent and substantial strength, harboring great ambition to retain the championship. However, Jinan University, having prepared its troops and sharpened its weapons, is determined to compete for victory. Judging from yesterday's results, Central University may not necessarily defeat Jinan, which has a good chance of winning. The following is a description of the championship situation:

—Track and Field Championship—

Central University Tense. Although Central University ranked first in yesterday's scoring, it only led Jinan by three points. Central's biggest failure was in the long jump. Zhao Rugong committed two fouls and then abandoned his third attempt, resulting in the complete loss of one of their most promising athletes.

World Olympic Games

—1936 in Germany—

Next Year in the United States—Japan Will Request to Hold It in Japan

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 14th. The World Olympic Games Committee decided today that the 1936 World Olympic Games will be held in Berlin, Germany. According to the committee, it is held every four years. Next year it will be held in Matsuno, USA. For the 1940 Games, it is said that Japan will request to hold it in Tokyo.

Chih Tze Celebrates Jiangnan University Basketball Championship

Twelve-Mile Race

—To be Held at 8 AM Tomorrow—

Revised Route

Rules and Penalties Decided

Expanded Prize List

List of Racers Announced

The highly anticipated twelve-mile Chinese race is scheduled to be held at 8 a.m. tomorrow. The following are the important updates obtained yesterday:

Revised Route

The route initially set by the association had the final section going straight to the athletic field from Lafayette Road. However, after investigation, Lafayette Road is currently under repair. The French Chief Inspector is concerned that the large number of spectators may hinder the racers. He requested the association's consent to change to a route of the same distance. The association specially sent Shi Youhui and Yao Wenhui yesterday afternoon to negotiate with the French Chief Inspector. The Chief Inspector first expressed his support and explained the road repair situation, requesting a change to Fulu Li Road leading directly to the athletic field. Shi and Yao agreed (see route map for details). The Chief Inspector also said that he would send a large number of police officers to protect the route.

Rules and Penalties Decided

The association convened a meeting of referees at 5:30 p.m. yesterday to decide on the penalties, as follows: (1) The referees will be assigned by the chief referee to different sections of the route, depending on the number of racers, to issue warnings and penalties, record the number of violations, and submit them to the chief referee for review. (2) If there are too many guides, hindering the progress of the racers, it is proposed to have them introduced in sections: racers numbered 1 to 150 should wait at the intersection of Wujiao Chang, and racers numbered 151 to 249 should wait at the entrance of Zhaofeng Garden. (3) Guides are not allowed to leave the racer they are guiding on the route and must follow the instructions of the referees at all times. (4) If other racers pass the racer being guided, the guide must give way and not deliberately obstruct them. Otherwise, the racer being guided will receive a warning. (5) Guides must stop at the intersection of Luban Road and take another route directly into the athletic field to prepare clothes for the racer to wear and are not allowed to enter or linger again. (6) All racers must gather at 7:30 a.m. on the 17th for roll call and departure. (7) Performers must wear blue short-sleeved shirts worn by the youth, without the need to wear numbers, but with a national flag on their chest. Guides are exempt to avoid congestion.

Expanded Prize List

The association originally planned to award prizes to ten people. Recently, due to the large number of prizes donated by various sectors, it was decided to distribute all prizes as much as possible to encourage the racers.

Shanghai Second Sino-Western Middle School Sports Meet

Men's First Place… Western Children's and Hanbury

Women's First Place… Western Children's Public School

The Shanghai Second Sino-Western Middle School Joint Sports Meet was held at Shen Park yesterday afternoon starting at 1:30 p.m. There were 15 participating Chinese and Western schools, with 152 male students and 49 female students. The program was extensive and complex. Chinese staff members included Ni Xiaoben and Le Xiurong. Kuang Fuzhu awarded the prizes. The rankings of each school are as follows: The scoring method for each school was 8 points for first place, 5 points for second place, 3 points for third place, and 1 point for fourth place. The competition results were: Men's Schools: 1st Place: Western Children's and Hanbury, 114.5 points; 2nd Place: American Children's Public School, 73 points; 3rd Place: Nie Zhongcheng Public School, 46.5 points; 4th Place: Chinese Children's Public School, 46 points. Women's Schools: 1st Place: Western Children's Public School, 74 points; 2nd Place: American Children's Public School, 70 points; 3rd Place: Hanbury, 21 points; 4th Place: Red Church School, 15 points.

Chinese Classics Research Association Establishes Correspondence Course

Since the Chinese Classics Research Association opened the Chinese Classics Correspondence Research Society, the number of people who have registered to join the Society has now exceeded the quota. Ma Zhe's Proof of the Nine-Point Circle Published

Ma Suda from Yongjia, based on his more than ten years of research experience and teaching experience, intends to publish several kinds of mathematical series. He has now completed and published "The Proof of the Nine-Point Circle." The book classifies and explains 726,017 kinds of proofs in detail, which is not seen in ordinary teaching books. Wu Zaiyuan, director of the Mathematics Department of Datong, said that his solutions and proofs are novel and the reasoning is easy to understand, which is not only for secondary school students to study, but also a good reference book for those who love mathematics and physics. It is said that the consignment office is Datong Bookstore on Sima Road. Mail orders can be directly sent to the Mathematics and Physics Research Society at No. 12, Yideli, Penglai Road, Ximen, Shanghai.

Local News

Yesterday's Held Hygiene Movement Week

First Day's Situation

Yesterday was the first day of the Shanghai Municipal Seventh Hygiene Movement Week. The Public Security Bureau specially ordered the head patrolmen of each district to supervise the sanitation workers at dawn to conduct a thorough cleaning in the city. The Municipal Health Bureau, regarding the publicity and implementation work of each section, advanced concurrently and was extraordinarily busy. The yesterday's situation is compiled as follows:

Citywide Cleanup　The central government stipulated yesterday (the

15th) as the national city and county cleanup day. After receiving the order, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau specially notified the 29 district police stations in the city and countryside a few days ago to urge the sanitation patrolmen to carry out cleaning and sweeping yesterday. More than 500 sanitation workers intensified sweeping as soon as it dawned. By 9 a.m., the main roads of the city were already presenting a clean road surface. At 12 noon and 3 p.m., the urban districts were still supervised by the sanitation patrolmen to continue sweeping. It is also heard that in addition to the special cleanup on the day stipulated by the central government (i.e., yesterday), the Municipal Public Security Bureau will strictly supervise the cleaning work from the 16th to the 21st. On one hand, each patrolman is responsible for rectification, and on the other hand, the bureau's special commissioner goes to the main roads and avenues of each district to investigate and observe, it is said.

Generality of Slogans　The day before yesterday, the Municipal Health

Bureau sent personnel to lead workers to post wall slogans in various districts of the north and south cities. Hygiene movement slogan strips in red and green characters and cholera posters on the walls of main roads, avenues, and near tram stops can be seen everywhere by passersby. The key points are recorded as follows: "Boil water before drinking, never drink raw water to avoid cholera," "Do not buy and eat exposed food and cut and sold melons and fruits," "To avoid cholera, get a vaccination quickly," "Pay attention to public health and cultivate a healthy nation," "Do not spit or urinate anywhere," etc. For the sake of widespread publicity, the bureau will continue to post these wall slogans and cholera pictures today (the 16th). The rickshaw association is responsible for the slogans posted on the rickshaw frames and forwards them to each rickshaw company to post on the frames. They have been found in the city yesterday, but only in a few places. The bureau believes that the hygiene slogans posted on rickshaws last year were not earnestly implemented, so this year it supervised the association to intensify implementation and rush to paste them widely on the 17th and 18th. At the same time, the bureau sent personnel to use trams, buses, and long-distance buses to post them. On the 19th and 20th, they were specially posted on telegraph poles.

Busy Vaccinations at the North Station　The health

department of the two railway administrations has expanded prevention work since the 15th. It specially cooperated with the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau to jointly run a free cholera vaccination station at the Shanghai North Railway Station, specializing in advising passengers from other places coming to Shanghai to get free cholera vaccine injections. It has been open since 8 a.m. yesterday. Medical officers and nurses dispatched by the railway bureau and medical staff dispatched by the Health Bureau set up tables and chairs outside the first and second-class waiting rooms inside the North Railway Station to cooperate in handling. From 8 a.m. to 6 p.m., cholera vaccine injections have been given to hundreds of passengers.

Departure Team This Morning　This morning (the 16th), a

team of doctors and nurses were dispatched to various municipal primary schools in the north and south cities to administer cholera vaccinations. The schools they went to include Municipal Xunyu, Mingzong, Cangji, Hubei, Gongshang, Dexin, Xinmin, and other primary schools.

Slow Vaccinations in Shantytowns　The shantytown areas in the city

are very numerous. The Health Bureau pays great attention to the hygiene of shantytown residents and the poor. From May 1st to yesterday, doctors have been vaccinating shantytown residents and children with cowpox vaccine every day. As of yesterday, a total of 20,297 people have been vaccinated. From November 1st last year to yesterday, a total of 181,329 people have been vaccinated. Although doctors went to shantytown residences yesterday to advise on cholera vaccinations, the poor often said "the weather is not hot yet" as a pretext. The doctors earnestly advised, but only a few responded to the vaccinations. Now the bureau has decided to implement compulsory vaccinations from the 20th. The period for vaccinations in shantytowns was previously stipulated by the bureau to be from May 1st to the turn of August and September, it is said.

Two Large Yellow Umbrellas　The Health Bureau specially made two large yellow

umbrellas, with a canopy length diameter of about eight feet and a bamboo handle more than ten feet long, painted with red slogans, for doctors and nurses to use to shield from the sun when going to shantytowns to administer vaccinations.

Public Notice from the Health Bureau　Hu

Hongji, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, issued a public notice yesterday, which was posted on the sides of various main roads, attached with various hygiene slogans. The public notice includes eight key points: (1) Everyone should get cholera vaccinations to prevent cholera; (2) Boil water before drinking, never drink raw water to avoid cholera; (3) Do not buy and eat exposed food and cut and sold melons and fruits; (4) Do not spit or urinate anywhere; (5) Everyone should pay attention to personal hygiene; (6) Everyone should maintain public hygiene; (7) If you are sick, you should see a doctor, do not be superstitious about seeking gods and taking elixir; (8) Maintain street cleanliness, do not step on it at will. The Situation in Shanghai County　Various agencies under Shanghai County

held a meeting at Maqiao in Puxi at 10 a.m. yesterday. Fu Dianying of the County Government, Jiang Yanchou, Tao Yishan, Gong of the Construction Bureau, She of the Education Bureau, Wang Chengyao of the Sixth District of the County, and hundreds of people from all walks of life attended. First, a meeting was held at Maqiao Qiangshu School, chaired by Wang Chengyao. After performing the rituals, the chairman first reported on the significance of the hygiene movement, followed by speeches by various officials. After the meeting, a photo was taken, and then the team marched in a parade. Each official held a broom and swept along the way. Hygiene slogans were posted everywhere, which was quite a grand occasion for a while.

The Situation in Baoshan County　Qiu Ming,

the magistrate of Baoshan County, convened more than 1,000 people from various agencies, groups, schools, and the public at the People's Assembly Hall at 1 p.m. yesterday to hold a grand cleanup and hygiene movement meeting. Magistrate Qiu chaired the meeting and reported on the significance of the cleanup and the elements of the hygiene movement and the relationship with the people's well-being in detail. Then representatives from various agencies and groups gave speeches one after another (the length of the speeches is omitted). Immediately afterwards, a parade set off, starting from the Assembly Hall, passing through Xin Street, out of the West Gate, passing along the city river, facing east, passing Xinglong Bridge, entering the West Gate, facing west to the Drum Tower, entering the North Gate, passing along Fengjia River, entering the East Gate, facing west to the Drum Tower, entering South Gate Street, passing through Miaonong, and returning to the People's Assembly Hall for dispersal. During the parade, leaflets were distributed along the way, slogans were shouted, and slogans were posted. The viewers blocked the road.

Yesterday, the Fresh Meat Industry Implemented Slaughter Cessation

Overnight Meat to Meet the Market

Talks with the Municipal Finance Bureau

The fresh meat industry in the north and south cities of the Chinese area, in opposition to the municipal government's direct collection of slaughter tax, held a meeting at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and resolved five conditions. On one hand, representatives such as Jin Guifu and Huang Jitang were sent to the capital to petition. It is learned that the authorities in the capital are holding a national conference these days and have no time to meet with the representatives, so Jin and others only submitted their petition and have already returned to Shanghai. However, the fresh meat shops are still insisting on the requirement that the slaughter tax be changed to a business tax and that the pre-slaughter and post-slaughter inspection fees be abolished. Starting yesterday, they have implemented a slaughter cessation and have asked a certain merchant to mediate. It is said that the meat sold yesterday and today is overnight meat slaughtered the day before yesterday.

The Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice that after the collection of the slaughter tax, it has been ten days, and the meat industry is still in dispute. Now we have obtained a detailed account of the situation from the bureau as follows: This bureau was ordered to take over the slaughter tax in the urban area, which was originally scheduled to be collected on May 1st. After the announcement, most meat businesses were waiting and watching. The initial intention of this bureau was that this tax revenue was transferred back to the city by the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office and was changed from contractor payment to direct collection. The meat businesses may not fully understand it, so they did not hesitate to send personnel to lead and guide them separately, hoping to avoid misunderstandings. Unexpectedly, after many days of delay, no one was seen buying tax tickets. When asked, the people in the meat business said that they originally wanted to comply with the regulations and pay taxes, but because the industry association asked them to wait for a solution, they dared not buy tickets alone, etc. Later, it was reported that a certain meat shop in the north of the city was carrying money to buy tax tickets, but was stopped halfway by colleagues, etc. This bureau repeatedly investigated the facts and believed that there must be someone manipulating it from behind. If strict enforcement is not carried out, it will inevitably become more and more serious. Unable to do otherwise, on the 9th of the month, each collection office was ordered to implement it in accordance with the regulations. On that day, the pigs slaughtered in the south and north of the city were not allowed to leave the factory because they had not purchased tax tickets. After 4 p.m., the meat shops in the south of the city purchased tickets from the collection office and took the pigs out of the factory. However, the meat shops in the north of the city still ignored it. After 5 p.m., the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter (already seen in the previous report). This bureau believed that the Chamber of Commerce was acting as a mediator and calculated the amount of tax owed. Since the Municipal Chamber of Commerce was responsible for recovering it, the collection office was immediately ordered to release the pigs stored in the factory first and temporarily count them before the 15th of this month. It was hoped that given time, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce would earnestly guide them and would not be deceived by villains again. On the 13th, it was suddenly seen in the newspaper that the Fresh Meat Industry Association had resolved to request the municipal government not to execute the buying of tickets and paying taxes, otherwise, they would unanimously close their businesses, etc. At the same time, it was reported that the number of pigs slaughtered in various slaughterhouses in the south and north of the city on the 14th of this month exceeded the usual number by one or two times, with the intention of striking. It is obviously visible that this bureau's takeover of the slaughter tax has not increased the burden on the meat industry. However, after repeated consultations against it, they did not hesitate to use the strike as a means of coercion. The reason for this is nothing more than a few villains who are playing tricks in order to restore the contractor system and achieve their desire to control and monopolize it. Everyone knows that the contractor system is easy to cause abuses. Under the revolutionary government, it cannot be allowed to exist forever, leaving a social stain. This bureau believes that directly handling all collections is to eliminate the interests of a few contractors and increase public revenue. In other words, the donations and taxes paid by the citizens are used as much as possible for municipal administration and are no longer pocketed by the contractors. Therefore, with this kind of reform determination, there is no slightest fear of difficulty. It is hoped that the meat merchants will not be fooled by a small number of people and suffer losses in vain, it is said.

Japanese Ship Caused Another Disaster

Sakimaru Collided with Xinming

In recent years, Japanese ships have been charging and colliding on the sea surface of our country, causing disasters from time to time. Although negotiations have been conducted, there have been few results. Now there is another incident of a Japanese ship colliding with a Chinese ship. We will urgently investigate and record what we have learned as follows: Xinming Was Hit　The China Merchants Bureau's northern line Xinming

ship was going from Shanghai to Tianjin this time. On the 13th, when the ship arrived at Dagukou, it was preparing to enter Tanggu and sail into Baihe to stop at Zizhu Forest. Suddenly, a Japanese merchant ship named Sakimaru came head-on. The captain of the Xinming ship tried to avoid the collision according to the sea route, but the Japanese ship directly crashed into the Xinming ship at close range. Fortunately, Xinming evaded urgently to avoid a major disaster. However, the stern of the ship had been hit, and the supports were damaged. Fortunately, the cargo and passengers were safe and sound.

Towed to Tianjin for Repairs　After Xinming was hit, the Tianjin branch

sent a ship to tow the ship into Tanggu and immediately reported to Tianjin Customs, which sent personnel to inspect and verify to prove that the Japanese ship caused the accident and should be fully responsible. After verification, workers were hired to repair it first. On the other hand, the ship reported the situation of the collision to the head office, opened a loss sheet, and demanded compensation from the Japanese ship.

Yixian Warship Trial Voyage to Minhang

The Speed Can Be 18 Miles Per Hour

Since the Yixian warship was launched, it has been nearly half a year, and the internal and external installations have been completed. It is scheduled to be compiled on June 1st and made

Yesterday's Trial Voyage of the Yixian Warship (Captured by Chunghua)

as the light cruiser of the First Fleet. It is learned that the ship departed at 7 a.m. yesterday, accompanied by Chief Supervisor Li Shijia, Captain Chen Hongtai of the ship, Deputy Director Chen Zaofan of the shipbuilding plant, and various supervisors. Overseas Chinese Unemployed in Jambi Cannot Return to China

China Merchants Bureau Has No Ship to Send

More than 350 unemployed overseas Chinese in Jambi are cut off from their livelihood and urgently need to be rescued and returned to China. The Chinese consul there telegraphed the Ministry of Industry, requesting relief. It is estimated that purchasing tickets and sending these overseas Chinese back to China will require at least more than 60,000 yuan. The ministry, lacking this huge amount, consulted with the Ministry of Communications and asked them to send a ship to carry them. Wang Boqun telegraphed Shanghai, ordering the China Merchants Bureau to send a merchant ship to Jambi to carry cargo and passengers, and to rescue unemployed overseas Chinese to return to China to avoid being stranded in foreign countries. The China Merchants Bureau has repeatedly planned this case and is very willing to do its best to rescue them. The result of the discussion was that there was no ship to sail overseas, and the power and heart were violated, so it was impossible to send them. Therefore, this fact was reported to the Ministry of Communications, requesting that another method be determined.

Postal Service Reduces Airmail Fees for Beijing and Tianjin

According to news from the Shanghai Post Office, starting today, all airmail to Beijing and Tianjin will have their special airmail rates reduced to the fees for one flight zone. For the convenience of the public, the section of airmail between Shanghai and Beijing passing through the Beijing-Shanghai section will be transferred by the Beijing-Shanghai night train.

Starting Today, National Customs Will Collect Unified Tax on Behalf

Tax Exemption Will Be Implemented Immediately

Restrictions on Business Tax on Cotton Yarn Merchants

The Ministry of Finance previously believed that the resident customs offices of the Unified Tax Administration should be abolished, so it expressly ordered the administration to abolish them uniformly from May 1st. All customs procedures for collecting the unified tax on behalf of the customs will be handled by the customs. After receiving the order, the Unified Tax Administration

Page 14

believed that the date of May 1st was too hasty, so it reported to the Ministry of Finance for approval and postponed it to today. The national customs will collect imported goods from foreign countries and non-unified tax areas that belong to the scope of the unified tax from today. The staff of the original resident customs offices of the Unified Tax Administration will be abolished from today. The Unified Tax Administration will specially give one month's salary to show compassion. In addition, Zhang Fuyun, Director of the Customs Administration, has replied to the administration yesterday that the exemption of native cloth from tax should be immediately ordered to the customs for immediate implementation. The business tax is not within the scope of the Unified Tax Administration. However, the collection of business tax on yarn mills in various places exceeds the original scope set by the central government and should be stopped by means of setting a regulation. Since merchants who buy and sell direct woven finished products are within the scope of exemption from the unified tax, they should be included in the business tax, it is said.

Yarn Stored Before February Should Be Absolutely Exempted from Unified Tax

The Yarn Association Requests the Ministry of Finance

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Yarn Mill Association telegraphed the Ministry of Finance about the issue of unified tax on yarn stored before February 1st, requesting absolute exemption in order to maintain commercial difficulties. The original telegram said, "Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, the unified tax exemption for yarn and cloth produced before February 1st. This association has repeatedly petitioned for an extension, which was only extended to April 15th. This inventory should not be subject to additional tax in terms of law and reason. Because the association does not dare not obey, it seems that yarn and cloth that has been shipped away from the manufacturing plant before the deadline should be allowed to pass through and cannot be asked about the ownership for the purpose of supplementing the tax or not. Otherwise, the deadline of April 15th is equivalent to setting up a false deadline. Recently, the unified tax bureaus in various provinces have been particularly demanding for this inventory, and merchants are therefore afraid, and yarn sales are completely stagnant, and the factory industry is almost impossible to maintain. We sincerely request that the ministry, thinking about commercial difficulties, quickly order the Unified Tax Administration to immediately cancel the original ownership restrictions on yarn and cloth that has been shipped away from the manufacturing plant before April 15th. The damage to the national treasury is limited, and the manufacturers are sincerely grateful for the gift. We cannot help but urgently await orders."

Negotiations on the Fire Disaster of Overseas Chinese in Tanah Grogot, Dutch East Indies

The Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission Requests the National Government to Allocate 30,000 Yuan First for Relief

On August 1st last year, a fire disaster occurred in Tanah Grogot, Dutch East Indies, which destroyed the wealth accumulated by overseas Chinese for generations, which is regrettable. However, the local government not only refused to offer a helping hand but also allowed the military and police to take the opportunity to loot. After the fire, they forced the overseas Chinese to relocate. Our innocent overseas Chinese, having suffered a fire disaster and been oppressed, were sorrowful and complained without a place to appeal. They telegraphed the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission one after another, requesting assistance. The Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission forwarded the request to the National Government, ordering the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to conduct serious negotiations and allocate funds for relief. It is heard that the Ministry of Internal Affairs convened the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Finance yesterday to discuss relief measures. As a result, the Ministry of Finance will first allocate 30,000 yuan for relief. As for the one-sided section, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will be responsible for handling it.

Recent News on Sino-American Shipping

Kawasaki Launches Regular Service: Following its collaboration with Toyo Kisen Kaisha, the Japanese firm Kawasaki Kisen Co. has added numerous new ships. It is now introducing new routes within the Pacific, establishing a regular service between China and America. It has been decided that starting from the 24th of this month, a dedicated Shanghai-San Francisco line will be inaugurated, deploying eight 8,000-ton vessels, departing every fourteen days. The first ship scheduled is the "Ryoyo Maru." Its business focus will be on aggressively competing for the transport of Chinese exports to Japan, while also carrying American lake silk.

Da Lai Implements Layoffs and Retrenchment: Due to business conditions and the current situation of numerous ships but a shortage of cargo, Da Lai Shipping Company is implementing a policy of retrenchment. Previously, twenty-eight employees, including office and dock personnel, were laid off. Now, following orders from the head office, further layoffs are being conducted. Four Western employees and three Chinese employees have been dismissed. It is reported that further layoffs are expected in the near future.

Bookbinding Industry Resumes Work Yesterday

Booksellers Reject Price Increases

After the strike by bookbinding workers in the city, they resumed work yesterday as ordered. The Booksellers Association held a meeting and firmly rejected price increases, making it difficult to resolve the wage issue. The details of the situation are described below:

Resumption of Work: After the bookbinding workers' union issued a notice for all workers to resume work, inspection teams set out yesterday morning in all directions (east, south, west, and north). Only the workers in the Zhabei area had not resolved the wage issue and refused to resume work. After repeated persuasion by the inspectors, over two thousand workers at more than one hundred and forty binding workshops fully resumed work around 9 a.m. As for the arrested workers, they were transferred from the judicial section to the Public Security Bureau yesterday. The union will submit a petition to the Social Affairs Bureau requesting their release on bail.

Booksellers' Meeting: The Booksellers Association held a committee meeting yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m., attended by thirteen people including Lu Feibohong and Cheng Xiechun. Chairman Lu Feibohong addressed the letter from the Bookbinding Association requesting an increase in bookbinding prices. It was decided that the increase in binding wages in the sixteenth year of the Republic [1927] was already substantial. In recent years, raw materials have been expensive, and business has been poor, making business increasingly difficult for booksellers, to the point of being unsustainable. In the past, many finished books were wholesaled to other areas, while few unbound sheets were. In the last four years, for the sake of saving on binding costs, other areas have gradually increased their wholesale of unbound sheets. It is feared that in the future, printing and binding will both be decentralized to the provinces and not concentrated in Shanghai. Judging from the facts of recent years, the number of lithographic printing presses has already decreased by thirty or forty units. Those that remain are struggling to find work to print. If this continues, the book industry and printing houses will suffer, and the bookbinding industry will also face ruin. Therefore, it is difficult to agree to the request for increased bookbinding prices. The Bookbinding Association will be notified immediately by letter.

Third Meeting of the Xin Anshan Support Association

The Shanghai Municipal Support Committee for the Xin Anshan Case held its third committee meeting yesterday at the Municipal Union Association. Zheng Chengqing presided. Shao Shixing and Zheng Chengqing reported on recent negotiations with the French authorities and the municipal government. Resolutions were passed on the following items: (1) Send a letter to the French consul, urging them to realize the situation and promptly negotiate the case with our authorities. Resolution passed. (2) Appoint negotiation representatives and determine negotiation principles. Resolution passed. Zheng Chengqing, Shao Baoxing, and Dong Xinqin were appointed as representatives. The negotiation principles are as follows: (A) Xin's disability is a fait accompli, and compensation for lifelong losses of at least 10,000 yuan is demanded. (B) The involved Western police officer should be dismissed and punished according to law. (C) The French authorities should formally apologize to our government. (D) Guarantee that similar incidents will not occur in the future. (3) Notify friendly nations of the facts and seek public judgment. Resolution passed. (4) Wire the five representatives from the city attending the National Assembly, urging them to supervise the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to conduct serious negotiations. Resolution passed. The meeting adjourned.

Central Government Explains That Rickshaw Pullers and Sedan Chair Carriers Cannot Form Unions

The municipal government instructed the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday regarding the prohibition of rickshaw pullers and sedan chair carriers from organizing unions. The directive stated that the Ministry of Industry had consulted on a case where the Anhui Provincial Department of Construction requested clarification on whether sedan chair carriers could form a union. The case had been referred to the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee for verification and reply. The reply stated that sedan chair carriers do not have an employer-employee relationship, provide their labor, and their work is not fixed in terms of time or location. They are completely the same as rickshaw pullers, and there is no need for them to organize a union. In addition to internal distribution, it is appropriate to consult with you for reference and to instruct your subordinates to take note. This directive is issued for the bureau to take note.

Italy Issues Prize-Winning Treasury Bonds

Those Interested Can Contact the Hua Yi Bank

According to news from the Hua Yi Bank in this port, the Italian government is issuing prize-winning treasury bonds on the market, with a total value of 400 million Italian lire. The terms are exactly the same as the previously issued and now expired treasury bonds, i.e., an annual interest rate of 5%, paid semi-annually, and repayment of principal after nine years. Prizes will be awarded annually by lottery, including two prizes of 1 million Italian lire each, two prizes of 500,000 Italian lire each, four prizes of 100,000 Italian lire each, and several prizes of 10,000 Italian lire each. The bonds will be issued from the 15th to the 26th of this month, with a net purchase price of 95. Those interested in learning more or purchasing the bonds can contact the bank at 16 Erma Road.

Request to Change Tooth Tax to Business Tax

Petition from the Various Industries Tax Regulations Association

The Tax Regulations Research Committee of the Shanghai Various Industries Associations submitted a document to the municipal government yesterday, requesting that the tooth tax be changed to a business tax. The case was based on a letter from the Chicken and Duck Industry Association stating that the draft regulations for business tax rates in the city, as formulated by the Bureau of Finance, did not mention the tooth industry. However, Article 21 of the revised Regulations for Business Tax in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces by the Ministry of Finance stipulated that the tooth industry should still follow its old regulations. In the past, during the tax assessment period, tooth tax permits in the city were all provincial property, and the tax was collected by the province, which was inconsistent with the authority of the municipal administration. The current draft business tax regulations in the city do not mention the tooth industry, but if the revised regulations of the Ministry of Finance are implemented, although business tax licenses will not be charged separately out of consideration for the difficulties of businesses, for the sake of unifying matters, the tooth industry should also be included in the city's draft business tax regulations and issued business licenses. This would benefit both the municipal administration and merchants. It is requested that the municipal authorities promptly include the tooth industry in the city's draft business tax regulations to comply with the law and benefit merchants. The Ministry-promulgated Outline of Business Tax, Article 6, stipulates that after the implementation of the business tax, all existing tooth tax permits and taxes in the provinces, slaughter taxes, etc., and other taxes similar to the business tax, should be abolished. Therefore, the association's request to change the tooth tax to a business tax is in line with the tax authority of the province and city and complies with the law. It is appropriate to prepare a document based on the facts and submit it to the higher authorities for review and transfer instructions to change the tooth tax to a business tax to unify authority, which is fair and convenient.

Various Industries Request Exemption or Reduction of Business Tax

Silk Factories: Shen Huachen, chairman of the Shanghai Silk Factory Association, sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance of the National Government in Nanjing yesterday, stating that the implementation of the business tax in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Hubei provinces will soon begin, and it is reported that the silk and cocoon industry is included in the scope of taxation, which contradicts the Outline of Business Tax and Supplementary Measures promulgated by your ministry. There are three reasons: Article 1 of the outline stipulates that "business tax will not be levied on items that have already been subject to special taxes levied by the central government." Cocoons are the raw material for silk, and a special tax has already been levied on the transportation and sale of raw silk. Therefore, this should be exempted, first. As for the location of the cocoon market, it only involves purchasing, and there is absolutely no sales business. According to your ministry's decree No. 5754, the Shanghai Various Industries Associations Tax Regulations Research Committee sent a telegram stating, "The agents who only buy and do not sell have no business income and are naturally not subject to taxation." The cocoon market is purely a purchasing agent and has no business income. Therefore, this should be exempted, second. Article 11 of the supplementary measures stipulates that "the first step of the transitional measures is to change the tooth tax permit to a business tax, and the tax rate will be levied according to the original amount of the tooth tax." Therefore, each cocoon market pays taxes and receives permits. This should be exempted, third. The silkworm cocoon season is about to begin. It is earnestly requested that your ministry issue a telegram to the governments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Hubei provinces to correct this and not include cocoon markets in the scope of business tax collection, so as to comply with the law and maintain commerce, which would be a great convenience.

Ham Industry: The Shanghai Ham Industry Association fraudulently sent a letter to the Tax Regulations Research Association, stating that ham and cured meats are the same type of food, and the collection of their business tax rate should be uniformly based on 0.2% to be fair and reasonable. Ham is made from the meat of pigs. Fresh pork is initially slaughtered, salted to become cured meat, and dried to become ham. Although the names are different, the substance is the same. Now, for the same type of food, cured meat and fresh pork are taxed at 0.2%, while ham is taxed at 1%. This is extremely unfair. I venture to submit my humble opinions as follows: (1) The process of making ham, from fresh meat to ham, involves only adding salt and the natural effects of air drying. There are no other materials mixed in. Since there are no other materials mixed in, ham and cured meat are essentially the same as fresh meat. This is one reason for the same taxation. (2) The raw material for ham is fresh meat, as mentioned above. Fresh meat spoils within one day in summer, and even in winter, it can only be preserved for a week. If salted to become cured meat, it can be preserved for three to five months. If dried and sun-dried to become ham, it can be stored for three years. Therefore, ham has a preservative effect and can be stored longer than fresh meat or cured meat. In other words, it embodies the virtues of thrift and frugality. This is a second reason for the same taxation. (3) To illustrate with vegetables, fresh green vegetables and radishes are equivalent to fresh pork. Pickled vegetables and radishes are equivalent to pickled meat. Dried vegetables and dried radishes are equivalent to dried meat like ham. Since there is no distinction between fresh, pickled, and dried vegetables, why should there be discrimination between fresh meat, cured meat, and ham? This is a third reason for the same taxation. In conclusion, the principle is clear. I urge your association to uphold justice and request the Ministry of Finance and the municipal Bureau of Finance to reduce the business tax on ham and collect it at the same rate as cured meat and fresh pork, to be fair and convenient for businesses. Respectfully submitted by the Shanghai Ham Industry Association to the Tax Regulations Research Committee of the Shanghai Various Industries Associations.

Guangji Ship Runs Aground on the Yangtze River

Hull Aground: The Guangji ship, which originally sailed to Wenzhou, was recently transferred by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, joining the Hankou-Yichang line. On the 14th, the ship was carrying cargo from Hankou to the Shayichang area when it ran aground on the Yangtze River about three miles from the Coal River. Cargo must now be unloaded before it can be towed.

Pilot Negligence: This incident was caused by the negligence of the pilot, causing the front of the ship to run aground on a shallow bank while the rear of the ship remained in the river. The water depth in that area is nine feet. It only needs to be lifted clear of the shallow bank to sail.

Dispatching Workers to Unload: Yesterday, the Shanghai office received the news and ordered the Hankou branch to quickly dispatch a small tugboat to unload the cargo from the Guangji ship to reduce the weight of the forehold. Then, tow it away. It should be rescued from the shallows in a day or two, and the hull is undamaged.

Recent Developments on the Two Railways

Since Luo Qinshan took office as the director of the two railways, he has been diligently rectifying the railway administration. Recently, it was found that more than 10,000 mu of land along the two railways had been rented to various households for farming. These tenants often owed rent for many years, which was detrimental to railway funds. He strictly ordered the property section of the general affairs department to actively rectify the situation, list the households that owed rent monthly, and order the rent collectors to collect rent on time. Those who failed to comply or colluded to conceal the situation would be punished. Also, due to the increasing number of passengers at the Shanghai North Station, Nanxiang, Jiangwan, and Taiwan stations, passengers often did not know the ticket prices, which was inconvenient. He instructed the transportation department to install price lists for each class of tickets next to each window of the ticket office for everyone's information. Twelve long benches were added to the platform at Nanxiang Station, and electric lights were installed in the awnings at Jiangwan and Taiwan stations, making it more convenient for passengers. In addition, a section of the platform at Wuxi Station was not covered by a wooden awning, making it difficult for guards to prevent theft. He instructed the engineering department to quickly build a shed to prevent theft. Furthermore, it was found that the lead seals on freight cars were not secure, often resulting in the theft of goods, which was detrimental to the reputation of the railway. He instructed the transportation department to review the situation and adopt new-style lead seals, similar to those used on the Pinghan and Xiang-E railways, to enhance security and ensure thoroughness. Luo has been with the railways for many years and is familiar with the situation on both lines. All measures are focused on convenience for passengers. With these improvements, passengers on the two railways will benefit significantly.

Highlights of the Screening of "Struggle of Love and Desire"

The sixth production of Lianhua Film Company, "Struggle of Love and Desire," is a major production written by the famous novelist Zhang Biwu, directed by Wang Cilong, and starring Zhou Wenzhu, Tang Tianxiu, Gao Zhanfei, and others. Filming has now been completed. A public screening was held yesterday morning at 10 a.m. at the Beijing Grand Theater, and over six or seven hundred people from all walks of life attended. The film's theme roughly focuses on love and desire, reflects the old and new ways of women, criticizes modern marriage systems, and summarizes family happiness. The entire plot is closely related to modern life, so its emotional appeal is extremely strong. Some audience members shed tears for the characters in the film. After the screening, everyone unanimously acknowledged it as an unparalleled masterpiece among domestic films. It is reported that the film is scheduled to premiere tomorrow, the 17th, at the Beijing Grand Theater, and seat reservations are very enthusiastic.

National Medicine Association: The day before yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau notified them to recommend two representatives to the bureau to answer questions in order to review the qualifications of the industry's union and determine whether the industry's union should exist. After receiving the order, the association convened a temporary executive committee meeting yesterday. It was resolved to publicly recommend two committee members, Zhuang Meitang and Cen Binghuang, to carry a summary and go as representatives. The association's summary to the Social Affairs Bureau is recorded as follows: "It is hereby verified that the drugstore clerks in this city are all in the position of commercial employees and are not allowed to organize unions according to law. The Training Department of the Central Executive Committee has explained in Instruction No. 12437, and the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee has decided in the 131st meeting. The original order and resolution are recorded later. The association has already submitted a written request to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce based on the above reasons, and requested the Ministry of Industry to review and handle it. It was stated in the Ministry's reply that if the pharmacy industry, the southern goods industry, etc., have no technical workers, but still organize unions, it is inconsistent with the law, so please consult the Shanghai Municipal Government for verification and handling. Now, upon receiving the notification from your bureau, the association was instructed to recommend two representatives to go to the bureau to answer questions in order to review the qualifications. We hereby express your bureau's respect for the central government's intention and adherence to the law. Therefore, it was publicly decided to recommend two committee members, Zhuang Meitang and Cen Binghuang, as representatives, carrying a summary, to report to the former case for training and guidance, and to present their views. We respectfully request instructions so that we may know how to follow them, which would be a great convenience. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau."

Local News II

Wang Zhenhuan Case: Kidnappers Committed Numerous Major Crimes

Three Cases of Kidnapping

Twelve Cases of Robbery

All Sentenced Separately Yesterday

Wang Zhenhuan, the young owner of Wang Yutai Tea Shop at No. 17 Julaida Road in the French Concession, was the victim of an attempted kidnapping. The criminals shot and killed Chinese Constable No. 2124 of the British Police Force and wounded Gatekeeper No. 1580. The criminals fled to No. 9 Zhengxingli, Beidi Road, entering through the front door and escaping through the back, abandoning a box cannon outside the back door of the house. Detectives arrived later, retrieved the weapon, and took it back to the police station to await arrest. This was previously reported. It is now known that Jin Jiulin, special detective inspector of the French Police, along with chief detective Li Yaolong, deputy detectives Qian Yumin, Mao Jingen, Zhang Ziying, and plainclothes detectives Zhou Buguang and Cai Jinzhang, discovered that the kidnappers were hiding at the Pingan Inn at No. 25 Pingjili Road. They proceeded to the inn the night before last without raising suspicion and arrested kidnappers He Yuren, Chen Xinggen, Zhu Debiao, Xue Mingshan, along with accomplice Pan Kaibang (the elder brother of the pirate Pan Kaiqu, a subordinate of Kaiqu with thousands of followers who specialize in looting on the sea outside Wusongkou), Miao Huaqing, and suspects Chen Gaoshan, Zhang Liansheng, Yu Peigui, Zhang Yishan, Tang Youting, Chen Deren, a woman named Jin Er Guniang, and Wang Sunshi, a total of fourteen individuals. They also seized a box cannon and a handgun and brought them to the police station. After interrogation by Western Detective Bao Ermao, He Yuren, Chen Xinggen, and Zhu Debiao confessed to plotting to kidnap Wang Zhenhuan and shooting and killing the Chinese constable. They also confessed that on February 8th of this year at 12:00 am, they attempted to kidnap Guangdong native Lin Weiqing, a head worker, at No. 55 Peikai'er Road in the Public Concession. On February 15th, they kidnapped Lu Mingsheng at the entrance of Leyuli on Yunnan Road, hiding the ransom note at No. 484 Fulililu. The family paid 32,000 yuan to redeem him, which was then divided among the kidnappers. In the past year and this year, they had also committed robberies in the French Concession, targeting the home of Cao Han at No. 22 Xiafei Road, the home of Ma Dongting at No. 20 Xiafei Road, the home of Cao Junda at No. 198 Pushi Road, the home of Zhang Maomao at No. 1 Lane 363 Kangti Road, Qian Fulai Nanyang Biscuit Company at No. 370 Houfuli, Bai'er Road, the home of Cao Sha II at No. 105 Fuka森 Road, Yongfeng Rice Shop at No. 180 Laoshenfu Road, the home of Wang Caimin at No. 5 Lane 94 Xiai Xian斯 Road (all robberies committed last year), the home of Zhang Jinquan at No. 455 Caishen Lane, Kangti Road, the home of Gao Yinfeng at No. 7 Tongkangli, Shengnv Yuan Road, the hosiery factory of Pan Sheng at No. 41 Anshunli, Kangti Road, and the home of Qian Longquan at No. 123 Meitaikong斯tuo Road, a total of twelve households. The order was given to detain them pending verification. Yesterday, they were sent to the French Court for prosecution. The Western Detective first reported the previous situation and presented the box cannon as evidence. Then, the plaintiffs complained about the circumstances of the robberies. Lu Liankui, a detective from the Chief Inspector's Office of the British Police Force, also filed a case, requesting that the four criminals, including He, be transferred for interrogation. He Yuren, Chen Xinggen, Zhu Debiao, and Xue Mingshan confessed to forming a gang to commit robberies and successively kidnapping victims, resisting arrest and committing violence. Pan Kaibang confessed that he was not present at the scene of the kidnappings, but that he had conspired to rob a certain store in Baxianqiao, which was unsuccessful, and was arrested by detectives. Miao Huaqing confessed that he was invited by Pan Kaibang to rob a certain store, and that he was not aware of the previous robberies. Chen Gaoshan, Zhang Liansheng, and others confessed that although they were acquainted with He Yuren and others, they did not know that they were thieves and requested a thorough investigation. Judge Zhu, the French Consul, sentenced He Yuren, Chen Xinggen, Zhu Debiao, and Xue Mingshan to five years in the Western Prison, to be deported after serving their time, and to be handed over to the mainland authorities for interrogation. They were first sent to the Public Concession Police Station for interrogation. Pan Kaibang was sentenced to three years, and Miao Huaqing to two years. Upon completion of their sentences, they will be permanently expelled from the Concession. Chen Deren, Jin Er Guniang, and Wang Sunshi were released as they were not involved. Chen Gaoshan and the other five were all expelled from the country. The seized box cannon and handgun were confiscated.

Pliers Used as Handgun

Li Buxin Specializes in Petty Crimes

Zhang Wenkui's Wife Saw Through the Fake

Zhang Wenkui, a local, 45 years old, operates a Yingyu Cigarette and Paper Store at No. 17 Nanjing Street in Nanshi. Around 9:00 pm the night before last, two robbers suddenly entered the store. Both were wearing blue cloth short shirts and pants and spoke with a Jiangbei accent. One robber brandished a black handgun, driving Zhang and his wife into a corner and warning them not to make a sound. The other robber then grabbed nine yuan in silver dollars and fourteen cents in small coins from the counter and fled out the door with the loot. As the robber holding the gun was about to escape, Zhang's wife realized that the black handgun was not real but a pair of iron pliers, with the handles hidden inside the sleeves. The middle section was being gripped, and the pliers head was exposed, resembling a handgun. It was originally intended to scare people. At this point, she felt a surge of courage and grabbed the robber from behind, shouting "Catch the robber!" Liu Xueqing, a watchman from the 24th patrol post nearby, and Yin Wanyou, a watchman from the 23rd patrol post, heard the commotion and arrived, managing to capture the robber. He was taken back to the First Precinct of the First District. During the preliminary interrogation by the station chief, the robber confessed his name was Li Buxin, 29 years old, from Funing, residing in Caonitang, Pudong. He claimed that he was experiencing financial difficulties, so he and his friend Ji Agen brought iron pliers to use as a fake handgun for intimidation. He did not expect to be arrested. He also stated that he and Ji had committed a robbery on a ship at Laiyi Wharf last month, obtaining five and a half yuan in silver dollars, and that ten days prior, they had also robbed a cigarette and paper store at the eastern end of Qinglong Bridge, obtaining five yuan in silver dollars and one hundred and eighty cents in small coins. Ji was also present. All the things they did were small-scale crimes, and the stolen money had already been divided and spent. As the matter involved robbery, he was ordered to prepare a document to be submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Two Westerners Accuse Each Other

A Major Dispute Over 200 Yuan

Involving Chinese Clerk Xuan Jinrong

Around 8:00 pm the evening before last (the 14th), a drunken Westerner took a train from Shanghai to Wusong and disembarked at Paotaiwan. He was staggering and claimed he wanted to go to the Feili Steamship Company to board a ship to Hankou. Chen Yinfu, a tea boy from the Seaside Hotel, was at the station picking up guests. The stationmaster Wu ordered Chen to take him to the Feili Company. Because it was late, there were no ships departing, so the company refused. Chen felt it was not his responsibility, so he returned to the hotel. Unexpectedly, after being rejected by the company, the Westerner ran around on the seaside until about 1:30 am yesterday morning. He went back to the Feili Company and knocked on the door. Xuan Jinrong, a Chinese clerk at the company, heard the noise and opened the door. The Westerner broke into the room and insisted on staying overnight. Xuan told him that this was not a hotel and he could not stay. Unexpectedly, the Westerner fell to the ground and fell sound asleep. The clerk had no choice but to let him be. When the Westerner woke up around 7:00 am yesterday morning, he got up from the ground and suddenly appeared alarmed, claiming that a wallet in his pocket, containing 200 yuan in banknotes, had disappeared. He accused Xuan of stealing it, and the two began arguing and were taken to the 7th District of the Public Security Bureau. Officer Cheng of the district interrogated them. The Westerner stated his name was Harder Peterson, 42 years old, originally from Norway but later an American citizen. He was currently the chief engineer of a Dutch steamship in Hankou. He came to Song from Shanghai last night and went to the Feili Company to borrow a room. He took out the 200 yuan in his wallet at that time and showed it to them. It was taken from Mitsui 洋行. 100 yuan was the company's public funds, and 100 yuan was for his personal use. They were all 10-yuan banknotes. He discovered the theft at 6:00 am this morning. Only Xuan saw it, so he concluded that Xuan had stolen it. Xuan stated that he was 60 years old and from Chongming. Around 8:00 pm last night, Chen Yinfu brought the Westerner to the company and said that he wanted to take a ship to Hankou. Because there were no ships, Mr. Zhang, the translator in the company, told me to close the door and ignore him. After the Westerner left, he came back to knock on the door at 1:30 am, insisted on staying, and fell asleep on the ground, refusing to get up. When he woke up at 7:00 am this morning, he falsely accused me of stealing 200 yuan and was very aggressive. While the interrogation was in progress, Mike, a British employee of the Feili Company, also filed a case, stating that Xuan Jinrong had been a Chinese clerk in the company for more than ten years and was very loyal. He could be held responsible for guaranteeing that he would not be a thief. Peterson broke into the company late at night without permission, which was illegal, so he filed a counterclaim and asked that it be investigated according to the laws of your country. Officer Cheng reviewed the confessions and found that the two Westerners' statements were inconsistent and the case was complicated. He immediately reported to District Chief Zhao Zezhou, who sent all the witnesses to the Public Security Bureau for legal action at 4:00 pm yesterday.

Mayor Zhang Serves as Honorary President

Held at the China-Japan Friendship Association Today
